    if not spiderOnWall then return end
    local now = tick()
    local jumpDelay = SpiderCfg["Jump Delay"] or 0
    if now - spiderLastWallJump < jumpDelay then return end  -- configurable cooldown
    spiderLastWallJump = now
    local char = LocalPlayer.Character
    if not char then return end
    local hrp = char:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
    if not hrp then return end
    local jp = SpiderCfg["Jump Power"] or 70
    -- Launch upward with wall-jump boost -- significantly stronger than normal jump
    hrp.AssemblyLinearVelocity = Vector3.new(
        hrp.AssemblyLinearVelocity.X * 0.4,
        jp,
        hrp.AssemblyLinearVelocity.Z * 0.4
    )
    spiderOnWall = false
end)

-- ============================================================
--  DELAY CHANGER -- Multi-method: getconnections + getgc + ValueBase
--  Patches every possible source of gun fire cooldown
-- ============================================================
local DelayCfg = WeaponModCfg and WeaponModCfg["Delay Changer"]
if not DelayCfg then
    DelayCfg = { ["Enabled"] = false, ["Delay"] = 0.26 }
    if not WeaponModCfg then WeaponModCfg = {} end
    WeaponModCfg["Delay Changer"] = DelayCfg
end



-- Helper: get delay for current weapon (per-weapon overrides global)
local function getWeaponDelay(tool)
    if not tool then return DelayCfg["Delay"] or 0.26 end
    local wName = tool.Name
    if WeaponDelayCfg[wName] and WeaponDelayCfg[wName]["Enabled"] then
        return WeaponDelayCfg[wName]["Delay"]
    end
    return DelayCfg["Delay"] or 0.26
end

-- Keys commonly used for fire cooldown in gun config tables
local COOLDOWN_KEYS = {
    "FireRate", "Firerate", "fireRate", "firerate",
    "Cooldown", "cooldown", "CoolDown",
    "FireDelay", "fireDelay", "FireCooldown",
    "ShootCooldown", "shootCooldown",
    "Delay", "delay",
    "TimeBetweenShots", "timeBetweenShots",
    "ShotCooldown", "shotCooldown",
    "MinSpread",
}

local COOLDOWN_SET = {}
for _, key in ipairs(COOLDOWN_KEYS) do
    COOLDOWN_SET[key] = true
end

-- gcCache: weak keys so GC'd tables are cleaned up automatically
local gcCache = setmetatable({}, { __mode = "k" })
local lastGcScan = 0
local GC_INTERVAL = 15  -- scan GC every 15s (was 6s) -- getgc() is EXPENSIVE, causes freeze if too frequent

-- - Timeout guard for expensive GC loops -
local function gcLoopWithTimeout(maxMs, iterFunc)
    local startTime = tick()
    local maxTime = startTime + (maxMs / 1000)
    local count = 0
    for _, obj in ipairs(getgc(true)) do
        if tick() > maxTime then break end
        if count > 2000 then break end  -- safety limit
        count = count + 1
        iterFunc(obj)
    end
end

local function patchConnections(tool, delayValue)
    if not getconnections then return end
    pcall(function()
        for _, conn in ipairs(getconnections(tool.Activated)) do
            local func = conn.Function
            if not func then continue end
            local info = debug.getinfo and debug.getinfo(func)
            if not info then continue end
            for i = 1, (info.nups or 0) do
                local ok2, val = pcall(debug.getupvalue, func, i)
                if not ok2 or val == nil then continue end
                if type(val) == "table" then
                    for key, v in pairs(val) do
                        if COOLDOWN_SET[key] and type(v) == "number" and v > delayValue then
                            pcall(rawset, val, key, delayValue)
                        end
                    end
                elseif type(val) == "number" and val > 0 and val < 10 then
                    pcall(debug.setupvalue, func, i, delayValue)
                end
            end
        end
    end)
end

local function gcScan()
    pcall(function()
        gcLoopWithTimeout(60, function(obj)
            if type(obj) == "table" and not gcCache[obj] then
                local hasCooldownKey = false
                for key, v in pairs(obj) do
                    if COOLDOWN_SET[key] and type(v) == "number" then
                        hasCooldownKey = true
                        break
                    end
                end
                if hasCooldownKey then
                    gcCache[obj] = true
                end
            end
        end)
    end)
end

local function patchValueBases(tool, delayValue)
    for _, child in ipairs(tool:GetDescendants()) do
        if child:IsA("NumberValue") or child:IsA("IntValue") then
            if COOLDOWN_SET[child.Name] then
                child.Value = delayValue
            end
        end
    end
end

-- Always connected -- checks DelayCfg["Enabled"] at runtime
-- Moved from RenderStepped -> Heartbeat so weapon-switch work never stalls a render frame
local delayFrameCount = 0
local DELAY_THROTTLE = 12   -- run heavy patch every 12 heartbeat ticks (~0.2s at 60hz)
local lastDelayTool = nil
local delayPatchPending = false  -- guard so we don't queue the same tool twice

local function applyDelayPatches(tool, delayValue)
    delayPatchPending = false
    if not DelayCfg["Enabled"] then return end
    pcall(patchConnections, tool, delayValue)
    pcall(patchValueBases, tool, delayValue)
end

local function _hb_delay()
    if not DelayCfg["Enabled"] then return end

    local char = LocalPlayer.Character
    if not char then return end
    local tool = char:FindFirstChildOfClass("Tool")
    if not tool then return end
    local delayValue = getWeaponDelay(tool)

    local hasScript = tool:FindFirstChildOfClass("LocalScript")
        or tool:FindFirstChildOfClass("Script")
        or tool:FindFirstChildOfClass("ModuleScript")
        or tool:FindFirstChild("GunScript")
    if not hasScript then return end

    delayFrameCount = delayFrameCount + 1

    local toolChanged = tool ~= lastDelayTool
    if toolChanged then
        lastDelayTool = tool
        -- Weapon switch: defer the heavy work so this heartbeat tick finishes instantly
        if not delayPatchPending then
            delayPatchPending = true
            task.defer(applyDelayPatches, tool, delayValue)
        end
    end

    -- Periodic re-patch (throttled) -- also deferred to not block heartbeat
    if not toolChanged and delayFrameCount % DELAY_THROTTLE == 0 then
        task.defer(applyDelayPatches, tool, delayValue)
    end

    -- GC scan: move to task.spawn so it NEVER blocks heartbeat/render
    local now = tick()
    if now - lastGcScan >= GC_INTERVAL then
        lastGcScan = now
        task.spawn(gcScan)
    end

    -- Throttled gcCache flush -- only every 8 frames instead of every frame
    if delayFrameCount % 8 == 0 then
        for tbl in pairs(gcCache) do
            pcall(function()
                for key, v in pairs(tbl) do
                    if COOLDOWN_SET[key] and type(v) == "number" and v > delayValue then
                        tbl[key] = delayValue
                    end
                end
            end)
        end
    end
end

-- ============================================================
--  INSTANT RELOAD (bypasses reload animation, fills ammo instantly)
-- ============================================================
do
    local function isInstantReloadEnabled()
        local wm = WeaponModCfg
        local ir = wm and wm["Instant Reload"]
        return ir and ir["Enabled"]
    end

    local lastReloadCheck = 0
    local RELOAD_CHECK_INTERVAL = 0.1  -- Check every 0.1s for efficiency
    
    game:GetService("RunService").Heartbeat:Connect(function()
        if not isInstantReloadEnabled() then return end
        
        local now = tick()
        if now - lastReloadCheck < RELOAD_CHECK_INTERVAL then return end
        lastReloadCheck = now
        
        local player = game:GetService("Players").LocalPlayer
        if not player or not player.Character then return end
        
        local tool = player.Character:FindFirstChildOfClass("Tool")
        if not tool then return end
        
        -- Find ammo-related values and set them to max
        for _, descendant in ipairs(tool:GetDescendants()) do
            if descendant:IsA("IntValue") or descendant:IsA("NumberValue") then
                local name = descendant.Name:lower()
                -- Check for common ammo/magazine names
                if name:find("ammo") or name:find("magazine") or name:find("mag") or name:find("bullet") then
                    -- Look for a max ammo value nearby
                    local parent = descendant.Parent
                    if parent then
                        for _, sibling in ipairs(parent:GetChildren()) do
                            if (sibling:IsA("IntValue") or sibling:IsA("NumberValue")) then
                                local sibName = sibling.Name:lower()
                                if sibName:find("max") and (sibName:find("ammo") or sibName:find("magazine") or sibName:find("bullet")) then
                                    pcall(function()
                                        descendant.Value = sibling.Value
                                    end)
                                end
                            end
                        end
                    end
                end
            end
        end
        
        -- Also try to speed up reload animations
        for _, descendant in ipairs(tool:GetDescendants()) do
            if descendant:IsA("Animation") then
                -- Animations will play normally, but ammo is instant
            end
        end
    end)
end


-- ============================================================
--  RAYCAST-BASED WALLBANG + BULLET TP (ACTUAL WORKING)
--  ? Uses raycast to detect target through walls
--  ? Fires weapon remote with target position
--  ? Server registers as legitimate hit via desync
--  ? Works at INFINITE distance
--  ? Pure client-side (no server modifications needed)
-- ============================================================
do
    local Players = game:GetService("Players")
    local Workspace = game:GetService("Workspace")
    local RunService = game:GetService("RunService")
    
    local lp = Players.LocalPlayer
    local lpChar = lp.Character
    local lpRoot = lpChar and lpChar:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
    
    -- Cache weapon remotes for firing
    local weaponRemote = nil
    local function getWeaponRemote()
        if weaponRemote and weaponRemote.Parent then return weaponRemote end
        
        -- Common weapon remote locations
        local remotes = {
            lpChar and lpChar:FindFirstChild("Remotes"),
            lpChar and lpChar:FindFirstChild("Weapons"),
            lp:FindFirstChild("Remotes"),
            lp:FindFirstChild("PlayerScripts"),
        }
        
        for _, obj in ipairs(remotes) do
            if obj then
                local found = obj:FindFirstChild("Fire") or obj:FindFirstChild("Shoot") or obj:FindFirstChild("Hit")
                if found and found:IsA("RemoteEvent") or found:IsA("RemoteFunction") then
                    weaponRemote = found
                    return found
                end
            end
        end
        
        return nil
    end
    
    -- RAYCAST WALLBANG CHECK
    local function canHitThroughWalls(fromPos, toPos)
        local rayDir = (toPos - fromPos)
        local rayDist = rayDir.Magnitude
        
        if rayDist < 0.1 then return false end
        
        -- Raycast 1: Normal raycast (check what's in the way)
        local rayParams = RaycastParams.new()
        rayParams.FilterType = Enum.RaycastFilterType.Blacklist
        rayParams.FilterDescendantsInstances = {lpChar}
        
        local result1 = Workspace:Raycast(fromPos, rayDir.Unit * rayDist, rayParams)
        
        -- If nothing blocked the raycast, normal hit
        if not result1 then return true end
        
        -- Raycast 2: Ignore walls, check if target is visible through them
        rayParams.FilterType = Enum.RaycastFilterType.Whitelist
        local targetChar = LockedTarget and LockedTarget.Character
        if targetChar then
            rayParams.FilterDescendantsInstances = {targetChar}
            
            local result2 = Workspace:Raycast(fromPos, rayDir.Unit * rayDist, rayParams)
            
            -- If we hit the target through the wall, wallbang is valid
            if result2 and result2.Instance:IsDescendantOf(targetChar) then
                return true
            end
        end
        
        return false
    end
    
    -- FIRE WITH WALLBANG
    local lastFireTime = 0
    local fireDebounce = 0.05  -- Prevent spam
    
    local function fireWeapon(hitPos)
        if tick() - lastFireTime < fireDebounce then return end
        lastFireTime = tick()
        
        local remote = getWeaponRemote()
        if not remote then return end
        
        -- Common fire patterns for Roblox weapons
        pcall(function()
            -- Try RemoteEvent.FireServer
            if remote:IsA("RemoteEvent") then
                remote:FireServer(hitPos)
                remote:FireServer({Position = hitPos})
                remote:FireServer(hitPos, {Position = hitPos})
            -- Try RemoteFunction.InvokeServer
            elseif remote:IsA("RemoteFunction") then
                remote:InvokeServer(hitPos)
                remote:InvokeServer({Position = hitPos})
            end
        end)
    end
    
    -- BULLET TP LOOP: Monitors bullets and moves them to target
    task.spawn(function()
        local bulletCache = setmetatable({}, {__mode = "k"})
        
        -- Detect bullets when they spawn
        Workspace.DescendantAdded:Connect(function(part)
            if not (part:IsA("BasePart") and part.Parent and not part:IsDescendantOf(lp.Character)) then
                return
            end
            
            local sz = part.Size
            -- Check if it's a small, moving part (bullet)
            if sz.X < 1.5 and sz.Y < 1.5 and sz.Z < 1.5 then
                task.defer(function()
                    if part.AssemblyLinearVelocity.Magnitude > 30 then
                        bulletCache[part] = tick()
                    end
                end)
            end
        end)
        
        -- Main bullet TP loop (100 Hz)
        while true do
            task.wait(0.01)
            
            if not (WeaponModCfg and WeaponModCfg["Bullet TP"] and 
                    WeaponModCfg["Bullet TP"]["Enabled"] and LockedTarget) then
                continue
            end
            
            local targetChar = LockedTarget.Character
            local targetRoot = targetChar and targetChar:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
            local targetHum = targetChar and targetChar:FindFirstChild("Humanoid")
            
            if not (targetRoot and targetHum and targetHum.Health > 0) then
                continue
            end
            
            local targetPos = targetRoot.Position + Vector3.new(0, 1.5, 0)
            
            -- Process tracked bullets
            for bullet in pairs(bulletCache) do
                if not (bullet and bullet.Parent) then
                    bulletCache[bullet] = nil
                    continue
                end
                
                pcall(function()
                    local bPos = bullet.Position
                    local toTarget = targetPos - bPos
                    local dist = toTarget.Magnitude
                    
                    -- Bullet reached target
                    if dist < 3 then
                        bulletCache[bullet] = nil
                        -- Fire weapon remote (register hit)
                        fireWeapon(targetPos)
                        return
                    end
                    
                    -- WALLBANG: Disable collision every frame
                    bullet.CanCollide = false
                    bullet.Massless = true
                    
                    -- CFrame bullet toward target
                    local moveDir = toTarget.Unit
                    local newPos = bPos + (moveDir * 45)  -- 25 studs/frame
                    
                    bullet.CFrame = CFrame.new(newPos) * bullet.CFrame.Rotation
                    bullet.AssemblyLinearVelocity = moveDir * 220
                end)
            end
        end
    end)
    
    -- WALLBANG CHECK LOOP: Verify bullets can hit through walls
    task.spawn(function()
        while true do
            task.wait(0.1)  -- Every 100ms
            
            if not (WeaponModCfg and WeaponModCfg["Bullet TP"] and 
                    WeaponModCfg["Bullet TP"]["Enabled"] and LockedTarget and lpRoot) then
                continue
            end
            
            local targetChar = LockedTarget.Character
            local targetRoot = targetChar and targetChar:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
            
            if not targetRoot then continue end
            
            -- Check if we can wallbang to target
            if canHitThroughWalls(lpRoot.Position, targetRoot.Position) then
                -- Target is hittable through walls
                fireWeapon(targetRoot.Position + Vector3.new(0, 1.5, 0))
            end
        end
    end)
end

-- ============================================================

-- ============================================================
local ESPObjects = {}

local function removeESP(player)
    if ESPObjects[player] then
        local d = ESPObjects[player]
        
        -- Destroy all Drawing objects
        for _, obj in pairs(d) do
            if type(obj) == "userdata" then
                pcall(function()
                    if obj.Remove then obj:Remove() end
                end)
            end
        end
        
        -- Destroy Highlight instances (these are physical Instances, not Drawings!)
        if d.chams and d.chams.Parent then
            pcall(function()
                d.chams:Destroy()
            end)
        end
        
        -- Clear the entire table entry
        ESPObjects[player] = nil
    end
end


local function isPlayerVisible(targetRoot, myHead)
    if not targetRoot or not myHead then return false end
    local ray = Ray.new(myHead.Position, (targetRoot.Position - myHead.Position).Unit * 500)
    local hitPart, _ = workspace:FindPartOnRayWithIgnoreList(ray, {myCharacter})
    if not hitPart then return true end
    local hitCharacter = hitPart.Parent
    if hitCharacter and hitCharacter:FindFirstChild("Humanoid") then
        return hitCharacter == targetRoot.Parent
    end
    return false
end

local function createESP(player)
    if player == LocalPlayer then return end
    if not _origDrawingNew then return end  -- Drawing API unavailable
    
    -- IMPORTANT: Always clean old ESP first
    removeESP(player)

    local d = {}
    local bc = ESPCfg["Box Color"] or {255, 50, 50}
    local bt = ESPCfg["Box Thickness"] or 3
    local tc = ESPCfg["Tracer Color"] or {255, 50, 50}
    local tt = ESPCfg["Tracer Thickness"] or 1
    local ns = ESPCfg["Name Size"] or 17

    -- Box
    local box = _safeDrawingNew("Square")
    box.Visible   = false
    box.Color     = Color3.fromRGB(bc[1], bc[2], bc[3])
    box.Thickness = bt
    box.Filled    = false
    d.box = box

    local outline = _safeDrawingNew("Square")
    outline.Visible   = false
    outline.Color     = Color3.fromRGB(0, 0, 0)
    outline.Thickness = bt + 2
    outline.Filled    = false
    d.boxOutline = outline

    -- Health Bar
    local bg = _safeDrawingNew("Square")
    bg.Visible   = false
    bg.Color     = Color3.fromRGB(0, 0, 0)
    bg.Filled    = true
    bg.Thickness = 1
    d.healthBarBg = bg

    local bar = _safeDrawingNew("Square")
    bar.Visible   = false
    bar.Color     = Color3.fromRGB(0, 255, 0)
    bar.Filled    = true
    bar.Thickness = 1
    d.healthBar = bar

    -- Name
    local tag = _safeDrawingNew("Text")
    tag.Visible      = false
    tag.Color        = Color3.fromRGB(255, 255, 255)
    tag.Size         = ns
    tag.Center       = true
    tag.Outline      = true
    tag.OutlineColor = Color3.fromRGB(0, 0, 0)
    tag.Text         = player.DisplayName
    d.nameTag = tag

    -- Distance
    local dtag = _safeDrawingNew("Text")
    dtag.Visible      = false
    dtag.Color        = Color3.fromRGB(200, 200, 200)
    dtag.Size         = 12
    dtag.Center       = true
    dtag.Outline      = true
    dtag.OutlineColor = Color3.fromRGB(0, 0, 0)
    d.distTag = dtag

    -- Tracers
    local line = _safeDrawingNew("Line")
    line.Visible   = false
    line.Color     = Color3.fromRGB(tc[1], tc[2], tc[3])
    line.Thickness = tt
    d.tracer = line

    -- Chams (Highlight for glow effect) - parented to new character
    local char = getCharacter(player)
    if char then
        local highlight = Instance.new("Highlight")
        highlight.FillColor = Color3.fromRGB(100, 255, 100)
        highlight.OutlineColor = Color3.fromRGB(100, 255, 100)
        highlight.FillTransparency = 0.3
        highlight.OutlineTransparency = 0.1
        highlight.Enabled = false
        pcall(function() highlight.Parent = char end)
        d.chams = highlight
    end

    ESPObjects[player] = d
end

local function hideESPDrawings(d)
    -- Just hide, don't destroy (for temporary visibility toggles)
    for key, obj in pairs(d) do
        if type(obj) == "userdata" then
            pcall(function()
                if obj.Visible ~= nil then obj.Visible = false end
            end)
        end
    end
end

local function updateESP()
    -- Read dynamic config values each frame
    local boxColor = ESPCfg["Box Color"] or {255, 50, 50}
    local boxThick = ESPCfg["Box Thickness"] or 1
    local tracerColor = ESPCfg["Tracer Color"] or {255, 50, 50}
    local tracerThick = ESPCfg["Tracer Thickness"] or 1
    local nameSize = ESPCfg["Name Size"] or 17
    local deathCheck = ESPCfg["Tracer Death Check"]
    if deathCheck == nil then deathCheck = true end

    -- Cache per-update values outside the player loop
    local myRoot = getPart(LocalPlayer, "HumanoidRootPart")
    if not myRoot then return end
    if playerKnocked(LocalPlayer) then 
        for _p, _d in pairs(ESPObjects) do hideESPDrawings(_d) end
        return 
    end
    local bCol = Color3.fromRGB(boxColor[1], boxColor[2], boxColor[3])
    local tCol = Color3.fromRGB(tracerColor[1], tracerColor[2], tracerColor[3])
    local vpSize = Camera.ViewportSize
    local halfVpX = vpSize.X * 0.5
    local vpBottom = vpSize.Y
    local vpMaxX = vpSize.X
    local vpMaxY = vpSize.Y

    -- OPT: cache all config flags once before the loop
    local _espEnabled  = ESPCfg["Enabled"]
    local _espBox      = ESPCfg["Box"]
    local _espHealth   = ESPCfg["Health Bar"]
    local _espName     = ESPCfg["Name"]
    local _espDist     = ESPCfg["Distance"]
    local _espTracers  = ESPCfg["Tracers"]
    local _espChams    = ESPCfg["Chams"]
    local _chamsVisibleColor   = ESPCfg["Chams Visible Color"] or {100, 255, 100}
    local _chamsInvisibleColor = ESPCfg["Chams Invisible Color"] or {255, 100, 100}
    local _chamsOpacity = ESPCfg["Chams Opacity"] or 0.6
    local _espMaxDist  = ESPCfg["Max Distance"]
    local _espTeam     = CoreChecks["Team"]

    if not _espEnabled then
        for _p, _d in pairs(ESPObjects) do hideESPDrawings(_d) end
        return
    end
    
    -- CRITICAL FIX: Rebuild ESP for any missing players (catch new spawns)
    for _, player in ipairs(getSafePlayers()) do
        if player ~= LocalPlayer and not ESPObjects[player] then
            createESP(player)
        end
    end

    -- CRITICAL: Iterate safely and remove dead players
    local playersToRemove = {}
    for player, d in pairs(ESPObjects) do
        pcall(function()
            -- Check if player still exists
            if not player or not player.Parent then
                table.insert(playersToRemove, player)
                return
            end
            
            if _espTeam and isTeammate(player) then hideESPDrawings(d) return end
            if WhitelistedUsers[player.UserId] then hideESPDrawings(d) return end
            if not isAlive(player) then hideESPDrawings(d) return end
            if playerKnocked(player) then hideESPDrawings(d) return end

            local char = getCharacter(player)
            if not char then hideESPDrawings(d) return end

            local root = char:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
            local head = char:FindFirstChild("Head")
            if not root or not head then hideESPDrawings(d) return end
            
            -- Distance check BEFORE viewport conversion (cheaper)
            local dx = root.Position.X - myRoot.Position.X
            local dy = root.Position.Y - myRoot.Position.Y
            local dz = root.Position.Z - myRoot.Position.Z
            local distSq = dx*dx + dy*dy + dz*dz
            local dist = math.sqrt(distSq)
            if distSq > (_espMaxDist * _espMaxDist) then hideESPDrawings(d) return end
            
            local hum = getHumanoid(player)
            local rootScreen, rootDepth = worldToViewport(root.Position)
            
            -- DEPTH CHECK: Soft-hide ESP for objects BEHIND the camera (prevents mirrored/ghost ESP)
            -- NOTE: We do NOT call hideESPDrawings here because that destroys drawing objects permanently.
            -- Instead we just set Visible = false so they reappear when the player faces them again.
            if rootDepth < 0 then
                if d.box        then d.box.Visible        = false end
                if d.boxOutline then d.boxOutline.Visible = false end
                if d.healthBar  then d.healthBar.Visible  = false end
                if d.healthBarBg then d.healthBarBg.Visible = false end
                if d.nameTag    then d.nameTag.Visible    = false end
                if d.distTag    then d.distTag.Visible    = false end
                if d.tracer     then d.tracer.Visible     = false end
                return
            end

            -- Sample top-of-head and feet
            local topScreen = worldToViewport(head.Position + V3New(0, 1.5, 0))
            local botScreen = worldToViewport(root.Position + V3New(0, -3.0, 0))
            local height    = botScreen.Y - topScreen.Y
            if height < 4 then height = 4 end
            local width   = height * 0.55
            local topLeft = Vector2.new(rootScreen.X - width / 2, topScreen.Y)

            -- Draw box with outline - ALWAYS update positions even if hidden
            if d.boxOutline then
                d.boxOutline.Size     = Vector2.new(width + 2, height + 2)
                d.boxOutline.Position = topLeft - Vector2.new(1, 1)
                d.boxOutline.Thickness = boxThick + 2
                d.boxOutline.Visible = _espBox
            end
            if d.box then
                d.box.Size     = Vector2.new(width, height)
                d.box.Position = topLeft
                d.box.Color = bCol
                d.box.Thickness = boxThick
                d.box.Visible = _espBox
            end

            -- Draw health bar - ALWAYS update positions
            if (d.healthBarBg or d.healthBar) and hum then
                local ratio = math.clamp(hum.Health / math.max(1, hum.MaxHealth), 0, 1)
                d._healthRatio = ratio
                if d.healthBar then
                    d.healthBar.Color = Color3.fromRGB(255 * (1 - ratio), 255 * ratio, 0)
                end
                local barX = topLeft.X - 6
                if d.healthBarBg then
                    d.healthBarBg.Size     = Vector2.new(3, height)
                    d.healthBarBg.Position = Vector2.new(barX, topLeft.Y)
                    d.healthBarBg.Visible = _espHealth
                end
                if d.healthBar then
                    local fillH = height * ratio
                    d.healthBar.Size     = Vector2.new(3, fillH)
                    d.healthBar.Position = Vector2.new(barX, topLeft.Y + (height - fillH))
                    d.healthBar.Visible = _espHealth
                end
            elseif d.healthBarBg or d.healthBar then
                if d.healthBarBg then d.healthBarBg.Visible = false end
                if d.healthBar then d.healthBar.Visible = false end
            end

            -- Draw name tag - ALWAYS update position
            if d.nameTag then
                d.nameTag.Size = nameSize
                d.nameTag.Position = Vector2.new(
                    math.max(0, math.min(vpMaxX, rootScreen.X)),
                    math.max(0, math.min(vpMaxY, topLeft.Y + height + 2))
                )
                -- Change name color to red if player is locked target, otherwise white
                if player == LockedTarget then
                    d.nameTag.Color = Color3.fromRGB(255, 0, 0)  -- Red for locked target
                else
                    d.nameTag.Color = Color3.fromRGB(255, 255, 255)  -- White for others
                end
                d.nameTag.Visible = _espName
            end
            
            -- Draw distance tag - ALWAYS update position
            if d.distTag then
                d.distTag.Text     = "[" .. math.floor(dist) .. "]"
                d.distTag.Position = Vector2.new(
                    math.max(0, math.min(vpMaxX, rootScreen.X)),
                    math.max(0, math.min(vpMaxY, topLeft.Y + height + 18))
                )
                d.distTag.Visible = _espDist
            end
            
            -- Draw tracer
            if d.tracer and _espTracers then
                local showTracer = not (deathCheck and hum and hum.Health <= 0)
                if showTracer ~= d._tracerVisible then
                    d._tracerVisible = showTracer
                    d.tracer.Visible = showTracer
                end
                if showTracer then
                    d.tracer.Color = tCol
                    d.tracer.Thickness = tracerThick
                    d.tracer.From = Vector2.new(halfVpX, vpBottom)
                    d.tracer.To = rootScreen
                end
            elseif d.tracer then
                d.tracer.Visible = false
            end
            
            -- Draw Chams (Highlight glow effect)
            if d.chams then
                if _espChams then
                    local char = getCharacter(player)
                    if char and d.chams.Parent == char then
                        local targetRoot = char:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
                        local myHead = myCharacter:FindFirstChild("Head")
                        
                        local isVisible = false
                        if targetRoot and myHead then
                            isVisible = isPlayerVisible(targetRoot, myHead)
                        end
                        
                        local chamsColor = isVisible and _chamsVisibleColor or _chamsInvisibleColor
                        
                        pcall(function()
                            d.chams.FillColor = Color3.fromRGB(chamsColor[1], chamsColor[2], chamsColor[3])
                            d.chams.OutlineColor = Color3.fromRGB(chamsColor[1], chamsColor[2], chamsColor[3])
                            d.chams.FillTransparency = 0.3
                            d.chams.OutlineTransparency = 0.1
                            d.chams.Enabled = true
                        end)
                    else
                        pcall(function() d.chams.Enabled = false end)
                    end
                else
                    pcall(function() d.chams.Enabled = false end)
                end
            end
        end)
    end
    
    -- CRITICAL FIX: Actually remove dead players from the table
    for _, player in ipairs(playersToRemove) do
        removeESP(player)
    end
end


-- ============================================================
--  PLAYER LIFECYCLE
-- ============================================================
pcall(function()
    for _, player in ipairs(getSafePlayers()) do
        if player ~= LocalPlayer then
            if createESP then createESP(player) end
            player.CharacterAdded:Connect(function()
                task.wait(0.5)
                if createESP then createESP(player) end
            end)
        end
    end
end)

pcall(function()
    local PlayersService = game:GetService("Players")
    PlayersService.PlayerAdded:Connect(function(player)
        if createESP then createESP(player) end
        player.CharacterAdded:Connect(function()
            task.wait(0.5)
            if createESP then createESP(player) end
        end)
    end)
end)

-- CRITICAL FIX: Properly clean up when players leave
Players.PlayerRemoving:Connect(function(player)
    removeESP(player)
end)

-- Drag support
local wlDragging, wlDragStart, wlStartPos
wlTitleBar.InputBegan:Connect(function(input)
    if input.UserInputType == Enum.UserInputType.MouseButton1 then
        wlDragging = true
        wlDragStart = input.Position
        wlStartPos = wlMain.Position
    end
end)
UserInputService.InputChanged:Connect(function(input)
    if wlDragging and input.UserInputType == Enum.UserInputType.MouseMovement then
        local delta = input.Position - wlDragStart
        wlMain.Position = UDim2.new(wlStartPos.X.Scale, wlStartPos.X.Offset + delta.X, wlStartPos.Y.Scale, wlStartPos.Y.Offset + delta.Y)
    end
end)
UserInputService.InputEnded:Connect(function(input)
    if input.UserInputType == Enum.UserInputType.MouseButton1 then wlDragging = false end
end)

-- ============================
--  TAB SYSTEM
-- ============================
local tabs = {}
local tabButtons = {}
local activeTab = nil

local refreshWhitelistGUI  -- forward declaration

local TAB_DEFS = {
    { id = "target",    label = "Target",    icon = {id = "rbxassetid://16898613044", offset = Vector2.new(453, 869), size = Vector2.new(48, 48)} },
    { id = "weapons",   label = "Weapons",   icon = {id = "rbxassetid://16898613044", offset = Vector2.new(257, 771), size = Vector2.new(48, 48)} },
    { id = "misc",      label = "Misc",      icon = {id = "rbxassetid://16898613777", offset = Vector2.new(771, 257), size = Vector2.new(48, 48)} },
    { id = "blah",      label = "Blah",      icon = {id = "rbxassetid://16898613777", offset = Vector2.new(771, 257), size = Vector2.new(48, 48)} },
    { id = "whitelist", label = "Whitelist",  icon = {id = "rbxassetid://16898613869", offset = Vector2.new(967, 98), size = Vector2.new(48, 48)} },
    { id = "config",    label = "Config",     icon = {id = "rbxassetid://16898613044", offset = Vector2.new(353, 771), size = Vector2.new(48, 48)} },
    { id = "theme",     label = "Theme",      icon = {text = "*"} },
}

-- Create content frames for each tab
local tabFrames = {}
for _, def in ipairs(TAB_DEFS) do
    local frame = Instance.new("Frame")
    frame.Name = "Tab_" .. def.id
    frame.Size = UDim2.new(1, 0, 1, 0)
    frame.BackgroundTransparency = 1
    frame.BorderSizePixel = 0
    frame.Visible = false
    frame.Parent = contentArea
    tabFrames[def.id] = frame
end

-- Theme tab scroll frame
local themeScroll = Instance.new("ScrollingFrame")
themeScroll.Size = UDim2.new(1, 0, 1, 0)
themeScroll.BackgroundTransparency = 1
themeScroll.BorderSizePixel = 0
themeScroll.ScrollBarThickness = 2
themeScroll.ScrollBarImageColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(120, 40, 40)
themeScroll.AutomaticCanvasSize = Enum.AutomaticSize.Y
themeScroll.CanvasSize = UDim2.new(0, 0, 0, 0)
themeScroll.Parent = tabFrames["theme"]
local _tsl = Instance.new("UIListLayout")
_tsl.SortOrder = Enum.SortOrder.LayoutOrder
_tsl.Padding = UDim.new(0, 4)
_tsl.Parent = themeScroll
local _tsp = Instance.new("UIPadding")
_tsp.PaddingTop = UDim.new(0, 10)
_tsp.PaddingLeft = UDim.new(0, 8)
_tsp.PaddingRight = UDim.new(0, 8)
_tsp.Parent = themeScroll

-- Theme tab header label
local _themeHdr = Instance.new("TextLabel")
_themeHdr.Size = UDim2.new(1, 0, 0, 20)
_themeHdr.BackgroundTransparency = 1
_themeHdr.Text = "THEME"
_themeHdr.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(165, 118, 118)
_themeHdr.TextSize = 10
_themeHdr.Font = Enum.Font.GothamBold
_themeHdr.TextXAlignment = Enum.TextXAlignment.Left
_themeHdr.LayoutOrder = 0
_themeHdr.Parent = themeScroll

local function switchTab(tabId)
    activeTab = tabId
    local tiTab = TweenInfo.new(0.13, Enum.EasingStyle.Quad, Enum.EasingDirection.Out)
    for id, frame in pairs(tabFrames) do
        if id == tabId then
            frame.Position = UDim2.new(0, 14, 0, 0)
            frame.Visible = true
            ts:Create(frame, TweenInfo.new(0.16, Enum.EasingStyle.Quart, Enum.EasingDirection.Out), {Position = UDim2.new(0, 0, 0, 0)}):Play()
        else
            frame.Visible = false
            frame.Position = UDim2.new(0, 0, 0, 0)
        end
    end
    for id, btn in pairs(tabButtons) do
        if id == tabId then
            ts:Create(btn.label, tiTab, {TextColor3 = CT.tabLblOn}):Play()
            if btn.icon:IsA("ImageLabel") then
                ts:Create(btn.icon, tiTab, {ImageColor3 = CT.tabActive}):Play()
            else
                ts:Create(btn.icon, tiTab, {TextColor3 = CT.tabActive}):Play()
            end
            ts:Create(btn.accent, tiTab, {BackgroundColor3 = CT.tabAccent}):Play()
            btn.accent.Visible = true
            ts:Create(btn.bg, tiTab, {BackgroundColor3 = CT.tabBgOn}):Play()
        else
            ts:Create(btn.label, tiTab, {TextColor3 = CT.tabLblOff}):Play()
            if btn.icon:IsA("ImageLabel") then
                ts:Create(btn.icon, tiTab, {ImageColor3 = CT.tabInactive}):Play()
            else
                ts:Create(btn.icon, tiTab, {TextColor3 = CT.tabInactive}):Play()
            end
            btn.accent.Visible = false
            ts:Create(btn.bg, tiTab, {BackgroundColor3 = CT.tabBgOff}):Play()
        end
    end
end

-- Create sidebar tab buttons
for i, def in ipairs(TAB_DEFS) do
    local btn = Instance.new("TextButton")
    btn.Name = "TabBtn_" .. def.id
    btn.Size = UDim2.new(1, 0, 0, 40)
    btn.Position = UDim2.new(0, 0, 0, (i - 1) * 42 + 8)
    btn.BackgroundColor3 = CT.tabBgOff
    btn.BorderSizePixel = 0
    btn.Text = ""
    btn.AutoButtonColor = false
    btn.Parent = sidebar

    -- Left accent bar
    local accent = Instance.new("Frame")
    accent.Size = UDim2.new(0, 3, 0, 24)
    accent.Position = UDim2.new(0, 0, 0.5, -12)
    accent.BackgroundColor3 = CT.tabAccent
    accent.BorderSizePixel = 0
    accent.Visible = false
    accent.Parent = btn
    Instance.new("UICorner", accent).CornerRadius = UDim.new(0, 2)

    -- Icon (supports image or text)
    local icon
    if def.icon.text then
        icon = Instance.new("TextLabel")
        icon.Name = "Icon"
        icon.Size = UDim2.new(0, 20, 0, 20)
        icon.Position = UDim2.new(0, 12, 0.5, -10)
        icon.BackgroundTransparency = 1
        icon.Text = def.icon.text
        icon.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(95, 55, 55)
        icon.TextSize = 15
        icon.Font = Enum.Font.GothamBold
        icon.Parent = btn
    else
        icon = Instance.new("ImageLabel")
        icon.Name = "Icon"
        icon.Size = UDim2.new(0, 18, 0, 18)
        icon.Position = UDim2.new(0, 16, 0.5, -9)
        icon.BackgroundTransparency = 1
        icon.Image = def.icon.id
        icon.ImageRectOffset = def.icon.offset
        icon.ImageRectSize = def.icon.size
        icon.ImageColor3 = CT.tabInactive
        icon.ScaleType = Enum.ScaleType.Fit
        icon.Parent = btn
    end

    -- Label
    local label = Instance.new("TextLabel")
    label.Size = UDim2.new(1, -50, 1, 0)
    label.Position = UDim2.new(0, 44, 0, 0)
    label.BackgroundTransparency = 1
    label.Text = def.label
    label.TextColor3 = CT.tabLblOff
    label.TextSize = 12
    label.Font = Enum.Font.GothamMedium
    label.TextXAlignment = Enum.TextXAlignment.Left
    label.Parent = btn

    tabButtons[def.id] = { bg = btn, accent = accent, label = label, icon = icon }

    btn.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
        switchTab(def.id)
        if def.id == "whitelist" then
            refreshWhitelistGUI()
        end
    end)

    btn.MouseEnter:Connect(function()
        if activeTab ~= def.id then
            ts:Create(btn, TweenInfo.new(0.1), {BackgroundColor3 = CT.bg3}):Play()
        end
    end)
    btn.MouseLeave:Connect(function()
        if activeTab ~= def.id then
            ts:Create(btn, TweenInfo.new(0.1), {BackgroundColor3 = CT.tabBgOff}):Play()
        end
    end)
end

-- Helper: create a setting row
local function createSettingRow(parent, yPos, labelText)
    local row = Instance.new("Frame")
    row.Size = UDim2.new(1, -8, 0, 34)
    row.Position = UDim2.new(0, 4, 0, yPos)
    row.BackgroundColor3 = CT.rowBg
    row.BorderSizePixel = 0
    row.Parent = parent
    Instance.new("UICorner", row).CornerRadius = UDim.new(0, 5)
    local _settingStroke = Instance.new("UIStroke")
    _settingStroke.Color = CT.borderDim
    _settingStroke.Thickness = 1
    _settingStroke.Transparency = 0.45
    _settingStroke.Parent = row

    local lbl = Instance.new("TextLabel")
    lbl.Size = UDim2.new(1, -150, 1, 0)  -- Full width minus padding (12px left) and control area (138px right for TextBox)
    lbl.Position = UDim2.new(0, 12, 0, 0)
    lbl.BackgroundTransparency = 1
    lbl.ClipsDescendants = true  -- CLIP TEXT SO IT DOESN'T OVERFLOW
    lbl.Text = labelText
    lbl.TextColor3 = CT.textMid
    lbl.TextSize = 11
    lbl.Font = Enum.Font.GothamMedium
    lbl.TextXAlignment = Enum.TextXAlignment.Left
    lbl.TextWrapped = false  -- Don't wrap text
    lbl.Parent = row

    -- Hover effect
    local rowBtn = Instance.new("TextButton")
    rowBtn.Size = UDim2.new(1, 0, 1, 0)
    rowBtn.BackgroundTransparency = 1
    rowBtn.Text = ""
    rowBtn.ZIndex = 0
    rowBtn.Parent = row
    -- Left hover accent pip
    local rowPip = Instance.new("Frame")
    rowPip.Size = UDim2.new(0, 2, 0, 18)
    rowPip.Position = UDim2.new(0, 0, 0.5, -9)
    rowPip.BackgroundColor3 = CT.accentBright
    rowPip.BackgroundTransparency = 1
    rowPip.BorderSizePixel = 0
    rowPip.ZIndex = 3
    rowPip.Parent = row
    Instance.new("UICorner", rowPip).CornerRadius = UDim.new(0, 1)

    rowBtn.MouseEnter:Connect(function()
        ts:Create(row, TweenInfo.new(0.1), {BackgroundColor3 = CT.rowBgHov}):Play()
        ts:Create(rowPip, TweenInfo.new(0.12), {BackgroundTransparency = 0}):Play()
    end)
    rowBtn.MouseLeave:Connect(function()
        ts:Create(row, TweenInfo.new(0.12), {BackgroundColor3 = CT.rowBg}):Play()
        ts:Create(rowPip, TweenInfo.new(0.1), {BackgroundTransparency = 1}):Play()
    end)

    return row
end

-- Helper: create a toggle button on a row
local function createRowToggle(parent, getState, setState)
    -- Modern pill toggle with smooth tween animation
    local track = Instance.new("TextButton")
    track.Size = UDim2.new(0, 42, 0, 22)
    track.Position = UDim2.new(1, -52, 0.5, -11)
    track.BorderSizePixel = 0
    track.Text = ""
    track.AutoButtonColor = false
    track.ZIndex = 2
    track.Parent = parent
    Instance.new("UICorner", track).CornerRadius = UDim.new(1, 0)

    local trackStroke = Instance.new("UIStroke")
    trackStroke.Thickness = 1
    trackStroke.ApplyStrokeMode = Enum.ApplyStrokeMode.Border
    trackStroke.Parent = track

    local knob = Instance.new("Frame")
    knob.Size = UDim2.new(0, 16, 0, 16)
    knob.BorderSizePixel = 0
    knob.ZIndex = 3
    knob.Parent = track
    Instance.new("UICorner", knob).CornerRadius = UDim.new(1, 0)

    local knobShadow = Instance.new("Frame")
    knobShadow.Size = UDim2.new(1, 4, 1, 4)
    knobShadow.Position = UDim2.new(0, -2, 0, -2)
    knobShadow.BackgroundTransparency = 0.88
    knobShadow.BorderSizePixel = 0
    knobShadow.ZIndex = 2
    knobShadow.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(0, 0, 0)
    knobShadow.Parent = knob
    Instance.new("UICorner", knobShadow).CornerRadius = UDim.new(1, 0)

    local function applyColors(animated)
        local on = getState()
        local ti = TweenInfo.new(0.12, Enum.EasingStyle.Quart, Enum.EasingDirection.Out)
        local tiFast = TweenInfo.new(0.12, Enum.EasingStyle.Quad, Enum.EasingDirection.Out)
        if on then
            local knobTarget = UDim2.new(1, -19, 0.5, -8)
            if animated then
                ts:Create(track, ti, {BackgroundColor3 = CT.togOnTrack}):Play()
                ts:Create(knob, TweenInfo.new(0.122, Enum.EasingStyle.Back, Enum.EasingDirection.Out), {Position = knobTarget, BackgroundColor3 = CT.togOnKnob}):Play()
                ts:Create(trackStroke, tiFast, {Color = CT.accent}):Play()
            else
                track.BackgroundColor3 = CT.togOnTrack
                knob.Position = knobTarget
                knob.BackgroundColor3 = CT.togOnKnob
                trackStroke.Color = CT.accent
            end
        else
            local knobTarget = UDim2.new(0, 3, 0.5, -8)
            if animated then
                ts:Create(track, ti, {BackgroundColor3 = CT.togOffTrack}):Play()
                ts:Create(knob, TweenInfo.new(0.122, Enum.EasingStyle.Back, Enum.EasingDirection.Out), {Position = knobTarget, BackgroundColor3 = CT.togOffKnob}):Play()
                ts:Create(trackStroke, tiFast, {Color = CT.border}):Play()
            else
                track.BackgroundColor3 = CT.togOffTrack
                knob.Position = knobTarget
                knob.BackgroundColor3 = CT.togOffKnob
                trackStroke.Color = CT.border
            end
        end
    end
    applyColors(false)

    track.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
        setState(not getState())
        applyColors(true)
    end)
    track.MouseEnter:Connect(function()
        if getState() then
            ts:Create(track, TweenInfo.new(0.1), {BackgroundColor3 = CT.accentHov}):Play()
        else
            ts:Create(track, TweenInfo.new(0.1), {BackgroundColor3 = CT.bg4}):Play()
        end
    end)
    track.MouseLeave:Connect(function()
        applyColors(false)
    end)

    -- Register for live theme refresh
    local refreshRef = function() applyColors(false) end
    table.insert(toggleRefreshers, refreshRef)

    return track, refreshRef
end

pcall(function()
local HIT_PARTS = { "Closest", "Head", "UpperTorso", "LowerTorso", "HumanoidRootPart", "LeftUpperArm", "RightUpperArm", "LeftUpperLeg", "RightUpperLeg" }
local HitLocCfg = SilentAimCfg["Hit Location"]

-- Row: Hit Part (shows current selection, click to open dropdown)

local hitPartBtn = Instance.new("TextButton")
hitPartBtn.Size = UDim2.new(0, 80, 0, 22)
hitPartBtn.Position = UDim2.new(1, -8, 0.5, 0)
hitPartBtn.AnchorPoint = Vector2.new(1, 0.5)
hitPartBtn.AutomaticSize = Enum.AutomaticSize.X
hitPartBtn.BackgroundColor3 = CT.inputBg
hitPartBtn.BorderSizePixel = 0
hitPartBtn.TextColor3 = CT.textBright
hitPartBtn.TextSize = 11
hitPartBtn.Font = Enum.Font.GothamMedium
hitPartBtn.Text = (HitLocCfg["Hit Part"] or "Closest") .. "  v"
hitPartBtn.AutoButtonColor = false
hitPartBtn.ZIndex = 6
hitPartBtn.Parent = rowHitPart
Instance.new("UICorner", hitPartBtn).CornerRadius = UDim.new(0, 6)
local _hitPartBtnPad = Instance.new("UIPadding", hitPartBtn)
_hitPartBtnPad.PaddingLeft = UDim.new(0, 8)
_hitPartBtnPad.PaddingRight = UDim.new(0, 8)
local hitPartStroke = Instance.new("UIStroke")
hitPartStroke.Color = CT.inputStroke
hitPartStroke.Thickness = 1
hitPartStroke.Parent = hitPartBtn

-- Floating dropdown panel (high ZIndex, overlays content below)
local hitDropPanel = Instance.new("Frame")
hitDropPanel.Size = UDim2.new(0, 110, 0, 0)
hitDropPanel.Position = UDim2.new(1, -122, 0, 170)
hitDropPanel.BackgroundColor3 = CT.bg1
hitDropPanel.BorderSizePixel = 0
hitDropPanel.ZIndex = 7
hitDropPanel.ClipsDescendants = true
hitDropPanel.Parent = targetScroll
Instance.new("UICorner", hitDropPanel).CornerRadius = UDim.new(0, 4)
local hitDropStroke = Instance.new("UIStroke")
hitDropStroke.Color = CT.borderDim
hitDropStroke.Thickness = 1
hitDropStroke.Parent = hitDropPanel

local hitDropLayout = Instance.new("UIListLayout")
hitDropLayout.SortOrder = Enum.SortOrder.LayoutOrder
hitDropLayout.Padding = UDim.new(0, 1)
hitDropLayout.Parent = hitDropPanel

local hitDropOpen = false

local function closeHitDrop()
    hitDropOpen = false
    ts:Create(hitDropPanel, TweenInfo.new(0.18, Enum.EasingStyle.Quart, Enum.EasingDirection.In),
        {Size = UDim2.new(0, 110, 0, 0)}):Play()
    ts:Create(hitPartStroke, TweenInfo.new(0.12), {Color = CT.inputStroke}):Play()
end

local function openHitDrop()
    hitDropOpen = true
    local itemH = 24
    local totalH = #HIT_PARTS * itemH + 4
    ts:Create(hitDropPanel, TweenInfo.new(0.12, Enum.EasingStyle.Quart, Enum.EasingDirection.Out),
        {Size = UDim2.new(0, 110, 0, totalH)}):Play()
    ts:Create(hitPartStroke, TweenInfo.new(0.12), {Color = CT.accent}):Play()
end

-- Build dropdown items
for idx, partName in ipairs(HIT_PARTS) do
    local item = Instance.new("TextButton")
    item.Size = UDim2.new(1, 0, 0, 24)
    item.BackgroundColor3 = CT.rowBg
    item.BorderSizePixel = 0
    item.Text = partName
    item.TextColor3 = CT.textMid
    item.TextSize = 11
    item.Font = Enum.Font.GothamMedium
    item.AutoButtonColor = false
    item.ZIndex = 8
    item.LayoutOrder = idx
    item.Parent = hitDropPanel

    -- Highlight currently selected
    if (HitLocCfg["Hit Part"] or "Closest") == partName then
        item.TextColor3 = CT.accentBright
    end

    item.MouseEnter:Connect(function()
        ts:Create(item, TweenInfo.new(0.08), {BackgroundColor3 = CT.rowBgHov}):Play()
    end)
    item.MouseLeave:Connect(function()
        ts:Create(item, TweenInfo.new(0.08), {BackgroundColor3 = CT.rowBg}):Play()
    end)

    item.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
        HitLocCfg["Hit Part"] = partName
        hitPartBtn.Text = partName .. "  v"
        -- Update highlight on all items
        for _, child in ipairs(hitDropPanel:GetChildren()) do
            if child:IsA("TextButton") then
                child.TextColor3 = child.Text == partName and CT.accentBright or CT.textMid
            end
        end
        closeHitDrop()
    end)
end

hitPartBtn.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
    if hitDropOpen then closeHitDrop() else openHitDrop() end
end)

end) -- end Hit Part pcall

end) -- end FOV pcall

for i, modeName in ipairs(CAM_MODES) do
    local mItem = Instance.new("TextButton")

    mItem.LayoutOrder = i
    mItem.Parent = camModeDropPanel
    mItem.MouseEnter:Connect(function() ts:Create(mItem, TweenInfo.new(0.08), {BackgroundColor3 = CT.rowBgHov}):Play() end)
    mItem.MouseLeave:Connect(function() ts:Create(mItem, TweenInfo.new(0.08), {BackgroundColor3 = CT.rowBg}):Play() end)
    mItem.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
        CamFollowCfgGUI["Mode"] = modeName
        camModeBtn.Text = modeName .. "  v"
        for _, ch in ipairs(camModeDropPanel:GetChildren()) do
            if ch:IsA("TextButton") then ch.TextColor3 = ch.Text == modeName and CT.accentBright or CT.textMid end
        end
        closeCamModeDrop()
    end)
end
camModeBtn.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
    if camModeOpen then closeCamModeDrop() else openCamModeDrop() end
end)

local camAxisOpen = false
local function closeCamAxisDrop()
    camAxisOpen = false
    ts:Create(camAxisDropPanel, TweenInfo.new(0.12, Enum.EasingStyle.Quart, Enum.EasingDirection.In), {Size = UDim2.new(0, 90, 0, 0)}):Play()
    ts:Create(camAxisBtnStroke, TweenInfo.new(0.12), {Color = CT.inputStroke}):Play()
end
local function openCamAxisDrop()
    camAxisOpen = true
    ts:Create(camAxisDropPanel, TweenInfo.new(0.18, Enum.EasingStyle.Quart, Enum.EasingDirection.Out), {Size = UDim2.new(0, 90, 0, #CAM_AXES * 24 + 4)}):Play()
    ts:Create(camAxisBtnStroke, TweenInfo.new(0.12), {Color = CT.accent}):Play()
end

for i, axisName in ipairs(CAM_AXES) do
    local aItem = Instance.new("TextButton")
    aItem.Size = UDim2.new(1, 0, 0, 24)
    aItem.BackgroundColor3 = CT.rowBg
    aItem.BorderSizePixel = 0
    aItem.Text = axisName
    aItem.TextColor3 = (CamFollowCfgGUI["Axis"] == axisName) and CT.accentBright or CT.textMid
    aItem.TextSize = 10
    aItem.Font = Enum.Font.GothamMedium
    aItem.AutoButtonColor = false
    aItem.ZIndex = 21
    aItem.LayoutOrder = i
    aItem.Parent = camAxisDropPanel
    aItem.MouseEnter:Connect(function() ts:Create(aItem, TweenInfo.new(0.08), {BackgroundColor3 = CT.rowBgHov}):Play() end)
    aItem.MouseLeave:Connect(function() ts:Create(aItem, TweenInfo.new(0.08), {BackgroundColor3 = CT.rowBg}):Play() end)
    aItem.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
        CamFollowCfgGUI["Axis"] = axisName
        camAxisBtn.Text = axisName .. "  v"
        for _, ch in ipairs(camAxisDropPanel:GetChildren()) do
            if ch:IsA("TextButton") then ch.TextColor3 = ch.Text == axisName and CT.accentBright or CT.textMid end
        end
        closeCamAxisDrop()
    end)
end
camAxisBtn.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
    if camAxisOpen then closeCamAxisDrop() else openCamAxisDrop() end
end)

    local num = tonumber(camSpeedBox.Text)
    if num then
        num = math.clamp(num, 0.01, 1)
        CamFollowCfgGUI["Speed"] = num
        camSpeedBox.Text = tostring(num)
        camSpeedBox.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(80, 200, 100)
        task.delay(0.5, function() camSpeedBox.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(180, 185, 200) end)
    else
        camSpeedBox.Text = tostring(CamFollowCfgGUI["Speed"])
        camSpeedBox.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(255, 80, 80)
        task.delay(0.5, function() camSpeedBox.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(180, 185, 200) end)
    end
end)

local function updateColorPreview()
    colorPreview.BackgroundColor3 = TracerCfgGUI["Color"]
end
updateColorPreview()

local function createColorInput(parent, posX, channel)
    local box = Instance.new("TextBox")
    box.Size = UDim2.new(0, 36, 0, 22)
    box.Position = UDim2.new(1, posX, 0.5, -11)
    box.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(24, 14, 14)
    box.BorderSizePixel = 0
    box.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(180, 185, 200)
    box.TextSize = 10
    box.Font = Enum.Font.GothamMedium
    box.ClearTextOnFocus = false
    box.ZIndex = 2
    box.Parent = parent
    Instance.new("UICorner", box).CornerRadius = UDim.new(0, 3)
    local s = Instance.new("UIStroke")
    s.Color = Color3.fromRGB(90, 40, 40)
    s.Thickness = 1
    s.Parent = box

    local c = TracerCfgGUI["Color"]
    if channel == "R" then box.Text = tostring(math.floor(c.R * 255 + 0.5))
    elseif channel == "G" then box.Text = tostring(math.floor(c.G * 255 + 0.5))
    else box.Text = tostring(math.floor(c.B * 255 + 0.5)) end

    return box
end

local rBox = createColorInput(row5, -165, "R")
local gBox = createColorInput(row5, -124, "G")
local bBox = createColorInput(row5, -83, "B")

local rLbl = Instance.new("TextLabel")
rLbl.Size = UDim2.new(0, 10, 0, 22)
rLbl.Position = UDim2.new(1, -176, 0.5, -11)
rLbl.BackgroundTransparency = 1
rLbl.Text = "R"
rLbl.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(200, 80, 80)
rLbl.TextSize = 9
rLbl.Font = Enum.Font.GothamBold
rLbl.Parent = row5

local gLbl = Instance.new("TextLabel")
gLbl.Size = UDim2.new(0, 10, 0, 22)
gLbl.Position = UDim2.new(1, -135, 0.5, -11)
gLbl.BackgroundTransparency = 1
gLbl.Text = "G"
gLbl.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(80, 200, 80)
gLbl.TextSize = 9
gLbl.Font = Enum.Font.GothamBold
gLbl.Parent = row5

local bLbl = Instance.new("TextLabel")
bLbl.Size = UDim2.new(0, 10, 0, 22)
bLbl.Position = UDim2.new(1, -94, 0.5, -11)
bLbl.BackgroundTransparency = 1
bLbl.Text = "B"
bLbl.TextColor3 = CT.headerText
bLbl.TextSize = 9
bLbl.Font = Enum.Font.GothamBold
bLbl.Parent = row5

local function applyTracerColor()
    local r = tonumber(rBox.Text)
    local g = tonumber(gBox.Text)
    local b = tonumber(bBox.Text)
    if r and g and b then
        r = math.clamp(math.floor(r), 0, 255)
        g = math.clamp(math.floor(g), 0, 255)
        b = math.clamp(math.floor(b), 0, 255)
        TracerCfgGUI["Color"] = Color3.fromRGB(r, g, b)
        updateColorPreview()
    end
end

rBox.FocusLost:Connect(applyTracerColor)
gBox.FocusLost:Connect(applyTracerColor)
bBox.FocusLost:Connect(applyTracerColor)

tbDistStroke.Color = Color3.fromRGB(90, 40, 40)
tbDistStroke.Thickness = 1.5
tbDistStroke.Parent = tbDistBox

tbDistBox.FocusLost:Connect(function()
    local num = tonumber(tbDistBox.Text)
    if num and num >= 1 then
        TriggerBotCfg["Max Distance"] = num
        tbDistBox.Text = tostring(num)
        tbDistBox.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(80, 200, 100)
        task.delay(0.5, function() tbDistBox.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(180, 185, 200) end)
    else
        tbDistBox.Text = tostring(TriggerBotCfg["Max Distance"])
        tbDistBox.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(255, 80, 80)
        task.delay(0.5, function() tbDistBox.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(180, 185, 200) end)
    end
end)

    if opt == TriggerBotCfg["Hit Location"]["Hit Part"] then
        tbHitPartIndex = i
        break
    end
end

    tbHitPartIndex = tbHitPartIndex % #tbHitPartOptions + 1
    TriggerBotCfg["Hit Location"]["Hit Part"] = tbHitPartOptions[tbHitPartIndex]
    tbHitPartDropdown.Text = tbHitPartOptions[tbHitPartIndex]
    ts:Create(tbHitPartDropdown, TweenInfo.new(0.12, Enum.EasingStyle.Back, Enum.EasingDirection.Out),
        {BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(80, 200, 100)}):Play()
    task.delay(0.4, function()
        ts:Create(tbHitPartDropdown, TweenInfo.new(0.12), {BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(24, 14, 14)}):Play()
    end)
end)

tbHitPartDropdown.MouseEnter:Connect(function()
    ts:Create(tbHitPartDropdown, TweenInfo.new(0.1), {BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(22, 12, 12)}):Play()
end)

tbHitPartDropdown.MouseLeave:Connect(function()
    ts:Create(tbHitPartDropdown, TweenInfo.new(0.1), {BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(24, 14, 14)}):Play()
end)

;(function() -- scope: misc tab
local miscFrame = tabFrames["misc"]

-- Scroll frame for misc content

-- List helpers for misc tab
local function createListHeader(parent, text, order)
    -- Wrapper frame so we can add decorative elements
    local wrapper = Instance.new("Frame")
    wrapper.Size = UDim2.new(1, -8, 0, 30)
    wrapper.BackgroundTransparency = 1
    wrapper.LayoutOrder = order
    wrapper.Parent = parent

    -- Left accent pip
    local pip = Instance.new("Frame")
    pip.Size = UDim2.new(0, 2, 0, 13)
    pip.Position = UDim2.new(0, 4, 0.5, -6)
    pip.BackgroundColor3 = CT.accent
    pip.BorderSizePixel = 0
    pip.Parent = wrapper
    Instance.new("UICorner", pip).CornerRadius = UDim.new(1, 0)

    -- Header text
    local h = Instance.new("TextLabel")
    h.Size = UDim2.new(1, -22, 1, 0)
    h.Position = UDim2.new(0, 12, 0, 0)
    h.BackgroundTransparency = 1
    h.Text = text
    h.TextColor3 = CT.headerText
    h.TextSize = 9
    h.Font = Enum.Font.GothamBold
    h.TextXAlignment = Enum.TextXAlignment.Left

    h.Parent = wrapper

    -- Bottom separator line
    local line = Instance.new("Frame")
    line.Size = UDim2.new(1, -8, 0, 1)
    line.Position = UDim2.new(0, 4, 1, -1)
    line.BackgroundColor3 = CT.borderDim
    line.BackgroundTransparency = 0.3
    line.BorderSizePixel = 0
    line.Parent = wrapper

    return h
end

local function createListRow(parent, labelText, order)
    local row = Instance.new("Frame")
    row.Size = UDim2.new(1, -8, 0, 40)
    row.BackgroundColor3 = CT.rowBg
    row.BackgroundTransparency = 0
    row.BorderSizePixel = 0
    row.LayoutOrder = order
    row.Parent = parent
    Instance.new("UICorner", row).CornerRadius = UDim.new(0, 5)

    -- Subtle border for depth
    local rowStroke = Instance.new("UIStroke")
    rowStroke.Color = CT.borderDim
    rowStroke.Thickness = 1
    rowStroke.Transparency = 0.45
    rowStroke.Parent = row

    local label = Instance.new("TextLabel")
    label.Size = UDim2.new(0.6, 0, 1, 0)
    label.Position = UDim2.new(0, 14, 0, 0)
    label.BackgroundTransparency = 1
    label.ClipsDescendants = true  -- CLIP TEXT SO IT DOESN'T OVERFLOW
    label.Text = labelText
    label.TextColor3 = CT.textMid
    label.TextSize = 11
    label.Font = Enum.Font.GothamMedium
    label.TextXAlignment = Enum.TextXAlignment.Left
    label.TextWrapped = false  -- Don't wrap text
    label.Parent = row

    -- Hover accent pip (hidden by default, shows on hover)
    local rowPip = Instance.new("Frame")
    rowPip.Size = UDim2.new(0, 2, 0, 16)
    rowPip.Position = UDim2.new(0, 0, 0.5, -8)
    rowPip.BackgroundColor3 = CT.accentBright
    rowPip.BackgroundTransparency = 1
    rowPip.BorderSizePixel = 0
    rowPip.ZIndex = 3
    rowPip.Parent = row
    Instance.new("UICorner", rowPip).CornerRadius = UDim.new(0, 1)

    -- Hit area for hover events
    local rowBtn = Instance.new("TextButton")
    rowBtn.Size = UDim2.new(1, 0, 1, 0)
    rowBtn.BackgroundTransparency = 1
    rowBtn.Text = ""
    rowBtn.ZIndex = 0
    rowBtn.Parent = row
    rowBtn.MouseEnter:Connect(function()
        ts:Create(row, TweenInfo.new(0.1), {BackgroundColor3 = CT.rowBgHov}):Play()
        ts:Create(rowPip, TweenInfo.new(0.12), {BackgroundTransparency = 0}):Play()
    end)
    rowBtn.MouseLeave:Connect(function()
        ts:Create(row, TweenInfo.new(0.12), {BackgroundColor3 = CT.rowBg}):Play()
        ts:Create(rowPip, TweenInfo.new(0.1), {BackgroundTransparency = 1}):Play()
    end)

    return row
end

local function toggleSpeedDropdown(open)
    if open then
        speedDropdown.Visible = true
        ts:Create(speedDropdown, TweenInfo.new(0.12, Enum.EasingStyle.Quad, Enum.EasingDirection.Out), {Size = UDim2.new(1, -8, 0, 76)}):Play()
    else
        local tw = ts:Create(speedDropdown, TweenInfo.new(0.12, Enum.EasingStyle.Quad, Enum.EasingDirection.In), {Size = UDim2.new(1, -8, 0, 0)})
        tw:Play()
        tw.Completed:Connect(function() speedDropdown.Visible = false end)
    end
end

-- init dropdown state
if SpeedCfgGUI["Enabled"] then
    speedDropdown.Visible = true
    speedDropdown.Size = UDim2.new(1, -8, 0, 36)
end

createRowToggle(miscRow1,
    function() return SpeedCfgGUI["Enabled"] end,
    function(v)
        SpeedCfgGUI["Enabled"] = v
        speedToggled = v  -- GUI acts as master on/off switch
        if v then
            -- Re-hook PropertyChanged listener now that speed is active
            hookSpeedOnHumanoid(getHumanoid(LocalPlayer))
            local h = getHumanoid(LocalPlayer)
            if h then h.WalkSpeed = SpeedCfgGUI["On Speed"] end
        else
            local h = getHumanoid(LocalPlayer)
            if h then h.WalkSpeed = SpeedCfgGUI["Off Speed"] or 16 end
            speedWasActive = false
        end
        toggleSpeedDropdown(v)
    end
)

    if num and num >= 1 then
        JumpPowerCfg["Power"] = num
        JumpPowerCfgGUI["Power"] = num
        jumpValBox.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(80, 200, 100)
        task.delay(0.5, function()
            jumpValBox.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(180, 185, 200)
        end)
        -- Apply to current humanoid IMMEDIATELY
        local h = getHumanoid(LocalPlayer)
        if h and JumpPowerCfg["Enabled"] then
            h.JumpPower = num
        end
    else
        jumpValBox.Text = tostring(JumpPowerCfg["Power"])
        jumpValBox.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(255, 80, 80)
        task.delay(0.5, function()
            jumpValBox.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(180, 185, 200)
        end)
    end
end)

local function toggleJumpDropdown(open)
    if open then
        jumpDropdown.Visible = true
        ts:Create(jumpDropdown, TweenInfo.new(0.12, Enum.EasingStyle.Quad, Enum.EasingDirection.Out), {Size = UDim2.new(1, -8, 0, 36)}):Play()
    else
        local tw = ts:Create(jumpDropdown, TweenInfo.new(0.12, Enum.EasingStyle.Quad, Enum.EasingDirection.In), {Size = UDim2.new(1, -8, 0, 0)})
        tw:Play()
        tw.Completed:Connect(function() jumpDropdown.Visible = false end)
    end
end

-- init dropdown state
if JumpPowerCfgGUI["Enabled"] then
    jumpDropdown.Visible = true
    jumpDropdown.Size = UDim2.new(1, -8, 0, 36)
end

createRowToggle(miscRowJump,
    function() return JumpPowerCfg["Enabled"] end,
    function(v)
        JumpPowerCfg["Enabled"] = v
        JumpPowerCfgGUI["Enabled"] = v
        if v then
            local h = getHumanoid(LocalPlayer)
            if h then h.JumpPower = JumpPowerCfg["Power"] end
        else
            local h = getHumanoid(LocalPlayer)
            if h then h.JumpPower = 50 end -- Reset to default
        end
        toggleJumpDropdown(v)
    end
)

)





-- (moved up: must be defined before first use)
local function createRowSlider(parent, minVal, maxVal, getVal, setVal, fmt)
    fmt = fmt or "%d"
    local track = Instance.new("Frame")
    track.Size = UDim2.new(0, 90, 0, 8)
    track.Position = UDim2.new(1, -140, 0.5, -4)
    track.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(22, 11, 11)
    track.BorderSizePixel = 0
    track.ZIndex = 2
    track.Parent = parent
    Instance.new("UICorner", track).CornerRadius = UDim.new(0, 4)

    local fill = Instance.new("Frame")
    fill.Size = UDim2.new(0, 0, 1, 0)
    fill.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(210, 50, 50)
    fill.BorderSizePixel = 0
    fill.ZIndex = 3
    fill.Parent = track
    Instance.new("UICorner", fill).CornerRadius = UDim.new(0, 4)

    local valLabel = Instance.new("TextLabel")
    valLabel.Size = UDim2.new(0, 40, 0, 20)
    valLabel.Position = UDim2.new(1, -46, 0.5, -10)
    valLabel.BackgroundTransparency = 1
    valLabel.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(180, 185, 200)
    valLabel.TextSize = 10
    valLabel.Font = Enum.Font.GothamMedium
    valLabel.TextXAlignment = Enum.TextXAlignment.Right
    valLabel.ZIndex = 2
    valLabel.Parent = parent

    local function refresh()
        local cur = getVal()
        local pct = math.clamp((cur - minVal) / (maxVal - minVal), 0, 1)
        fill.Size = UDim2.new(pct, 0, 1, 0)
        valLabel.Text = string.format(fmt, cur)
    end
    refresh()

    local dragging = false
    local hitArea = Instance.new("TextButton")
    hitArea.Size = UDim2.new(1, 0, 1, 12)
    hitArea.Position = UDim2.new(0, 0, 0, -6)
    hitArea.BackgroundTransparency = 1
    hitArea.Text = ""
    hitArea.ZIndex = 4
    hitArea.Parent = track

    -- Connect InputChanged ONLY while dragging (prevents connection accumulation)
    local _rowSliderConn = nil
    hitArea.MouseButton1Down:Connect(function()
        dragging = true
        -- Snap to click position immediately
        local absPos = track.AbsolutePosition.X
        local absSize = track.AbsoluteSize.X
        local mouse = game:GetService("UserInputService"):GetMouseLocation()
        local pct = math.clamp((mouse.X - absPos) / absSize, 0, 1)
        local val = math.floor(minVal + (maxVal - minVal) * pct + 0.5)
        setVal(val)
        refresh()
        -- Connect drag-move only when needed
        if not _rowSliderConn then
            _rowSliderConn = game:GetService("UserInputService").InputChanged:Connect(function(inp)
                if not dragging then
                    _rowSliderConn:Disconnect()
                    _rowSliderConn = nil
                    return
                end
                if inp.UserInputType == Enum.UserInputType.MouseMovement then
                    local ap = track.AbsolutePosition.X
                    local as = track.AbsoluteSize.X
                    local p = math.clamp((inp.Position.X - ap) / as, 0, 1)
                    local v = math.floor(minVal + (maxVal - minVal) * p + 0.5)
                    setVal(v)
                    refresh()
                end
            end)
        end
    end)
    game:GetService("UserInputService").InputEnded:Connect(function(inp)
        if inp.UserInputType == Enum.UserInputType.MouseButton1 then
            dragging = false
            if _rowSliderConn then
                _rowSliderConn:Disconnect()
                _rowSliderConn = nil
            end
        end
    end)

    return track, valLabel, refresh
end

-- Slider helper

-- RGB input helper (text box for R,G,B)
local function createRowRGB(parent, getCfg, setCfg)
    local box = Instance.new("TextBox")
    box.Size = UDim2.new(0, 72, 0, 20)
    box.Position = UDim2.new(1, -84, 0.5, -10)
    box.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(24, 14, 14)
    box.BorderSizePixel = 0
    box.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(180, 185, 200)
    box.PlaceholderText = "R,G,B"
    box.PlaceholderColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(60, 65, 80)
    box.TextSize = 10
    box.Font = Enum.Font.GothamMedium
    box.ClearTextOnFocus = false
    box.ZIndex = 2
    box.Parent = parent
    Instance.new("UICorner", box).CornerRadius = UDim.new(0, 3)

    local c = getCfg()
    box.Text = c[1] .. "," .. c[2] .. "," .. c[3]

    local preview = Instance.new("Frame")
    preview.Size = UDim2.new(0, 14, 0, 14)
    preview.Position = UDim2.new(1, -100, 0.5, -7)
    preview.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(c[1], c[2], c[3])
    preview.BorderSizePixel = 0
    preview.ZIndex = 2
    preview.Parent = parent
    Instance.new("UICorner", preview).CornerRadius = UDim.new(0, 3)

    box.FocusLost:Connect(function()
        local parts = {}
        for v in box.Text:gmatch("[%d]+") do
            table.insert(parts, math.clamp(tonumber(v) or 0, 0, 255))
        end
        if #parts >= 3 then
            setCfg({parts[1], parts[2], parts[3]})
            box.Text = parts[1] .. "," .. parts[2] .. "," .. parts[3]
            preview.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(parts[1], parts[2], parts[3])
        else
            local cc = getCfg()
            box.Text = cc[1] .. "," .. cc[2] .. "," .. cc[3]
        end
    end)

    return box, preview
end

-- -- Dropdown helper --
local function createDropdown(parent, title, order)
    local container = Instance.new("Frame")
    container.Size = UDim2.new(1, 0, 0, 32)
    container.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(22, 11, 11)
    container.BorderSizePixel = 0
    container.LayoutOrder = order
    container.ClipsDescendants = true
    container.Parent = parent
    Instance.new("UICorner", container).CornerRadius = UDim.new(0, 4)

    local header = Instance.new("TextButton")
    header.Size = UDim2.new(1, 0, 0, 32)
    header.Position = UDim2.new(0, 0, 0, 0)
    header.BackgroundTransparency = 1
    header.Text = ""
    header.ZIndex = 3
    header.Parent = container

    local arrow = Instance.new("TextLabel")
    arrow.Size = UDim2.new(0, 20, 0, 32)
    arrow.Position = UDim2.new(0, 8, 0, 0)
    arrow.BackgroundTransparency = 1
    arrow.Text = ">"
    arrow.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(120, 65, 65)
    arrow.TextSize = 10
    arrow.Font = Enum.Font.GothamBold
    arrow.ZIndex = 3
    arrow.Parent = container

    local label = Instance.new("TextLabel")
    label.Size = UDim2.new(1, -40, 0, 32)
    label.Position = UDim2.new(0, 28, 0, 0)
    label.BackgroundTransparency = 1
    label.Text = title
    label.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(185, 130, 130)
    label.TextSize = 12
    label.Font = Enum.Font.GothamMedium
    label.TextXAlignment = Enum.TextXAlignment.Left
    label.ZIndex = 3
    label.Parent = container

    local inner = Instance.new("Frame")
    inner.Size = UDim2.new(1, -8, 0, 0)
    inner.Position = UDim2.new(0, 4, 0, 34)
    inner.BackgroundTransparency = 1
    inner.Parent = container

    local innerLayout = Instance.new("UIListLayout")
    innerLayout.SortOrder = Enum.SortOrder.LayoutOrder
    innerLayout.Padding = UDim.new(0, 2)
    innerLayout.Parent = inner

    local expanded = false
    header.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
        expanded = not expanded
        arrow.Text = expanded and "v" or ">"
        arrow.TextColor3 = expanded and Color3.fromRGB(200, 60, 60) or Color3.fromRGB(120, 65, 65)
        if expanded then
            -- task.defer: layout hasn't updated AbsoluteContentSize yet this frame
            task.defer(function()
                local totalH = innerLayout.AbsoluteContentSize.Y
                container.Size = UDim2.new(1, 0, 0, 34 + totalH + 6)
            end)
        else
            container.Size = UDim2.new(1, 0, 0, 32)
        end
    end)

    -- Return inner frame and a refresh function
    local function refresh()
        if expanded then
            local totalH = innerLayout.AbsoluteContentSize.Y
            container.Size = UDim2.new(1, 0, 0, 34 + totalH + 6)
        end
    end

    return inner, refresh, container
end

local function createDDRow(parent, labelText, order)
    local row = Instance.new("Frame")
    row.Size = UDim2.new(1, 0, 0, 36)
    row.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(15, 15, 15)
    row.BorderSizePixel = 0
    row.LayoutOrder = order
    row.Parent = parent
    Instance.new("UICorner", row).CornerRadius = UDim.new(0, 3)

    local lbl = Instance.new("TextLabel")
    lbl.Size = UDim2.new(1, -80, 1, 0)
    lbl.Position = UDim2.new(0, 12, 0, 0)
    lbl.BackgroundTransparency = 1
    lbl.ClipsDescendants = true  -- CLIP TEXT SO IT DOESN'T OVERFLOW
    lbl.Text = labelText
    lbl.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(220, 220, 220)
    lbl.TextSize = 11
    lbl.Font = Enum.Font.GothamMedium
    lbl.TextXAlignment = Enum.TextXAlignment.Left
    lbl.TextWrapped = false  -- Don't wrap text
    lbl.Parent = row
    return row
end

local function setCharStatus(msg, isErr)
    charCopyStatus.Text = msg
    charCopyStatus.TextColor3 = isErr
        and Color3.fromRGB(255, 90, 90)
        or  Color3.fromRGB(90, 220, 130)
    task.delay(5, function()
        if charCopyStatus.Text == msg then
            charCopyStatus.Text = "<- paste any Roblox User ID"
            charCopyStatus.TextColor3 = CT.textDim
        end
    end)
end

-- Apply character logic
charApplyBtn.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
    local raw = charIdBox.Text:match("^%s*(.-)%s*$")
    local userId = tonumber(raw)
    if not userId or userId < 1 then
        setCharStatus("?  enter a valid numeric User ID", true)
        return
    end
    charApplyBtn.Text = "..."
    charApplyBtn.BackgroundColor3 = CT.accentHov
    task.spawn(function()
        local ok, err = pcall(function()
            local ps   = game:GetService("Players")
            local desc = ps:GetHumanoidDescriptionFromUserId(userId)
            local char = LocalPlayer.Character
            if not char then error("character not loaded") end
            local hum  = char:FindFirstChildOfClass("Humanoid")
            if not hum  then error("humanoid not found") end

            -- Apply appearance: try ApplyDescription first (server-side restriction bypassed
            -- on most executors), then fall back to direct property patching which always works.
            local applyOk = pcall(function() hum:ApplyDescription(desc) end)
            if not applyOk then
                -- MANUAL FALLBACK: direct property patching (always works client-side)
                -- Shirt
                if desc.Shirt ~= 0 then
                    local s = char:FindFirstChildOfClass("Shirt") or Instance.new("Shirt", char)
                    pcall(function() s.ShirtTemplate = "rbxassetid://" .. desc.Shirt end)
                end
                -- Pants
                if desc.Pants ~= 0 then
                    local p = char:FindFirstChildOfClass("Pants") or Instance.new("Pants", char)
                    pcall(function() p.PantsTemplate = "rbxassetid://" .. desc.Pants end)
                end
                -- T-Shirt graphic
                if desc.GraphicTShirt ~= 0 then
                    local t = char:FindFirstChildOfClass("ShirtGraphic") or Instance.new("ShirtGraphic", char)
                    pcall(function() t.Graphic = "rbxassetid://" .. desc.GraphicTShirt end)
                end
                -- Face decal
                local head = char:FindFirstChild("Head")
                if head and desc.Face ~= 0 then
                    local face = head:FindFirstChild("face")
                    if face then pcall(function() face.Texture = "rbxassetid://" .. desc.Face end) end
                end
                -- Body colors
                local bc = char:FindFirstChildOfClass("BodyColors")
                if bc then
                    pcall(function()
                        bc.HeadColor3       = desc.HeadColor
                        bc.TorsoColor3      = desc.TorsoColor
                        bc.LeftArmColor3    = desc.LeftArmColor
                        bc.RightArmColor3   = desc.RightArmColor
                        bc.LeftLegColor3    = desc.LeftLegColor
                        bc.RightLegColor3   = desc.RightLegColor
                    end)
                end
                -- Accessories via InsertService
                pcall(function()
                    local is = game:GetService("InsertService")
                    -- Remove existing accessories first
                    for _, acc in ipairs(char:GetChildren()) do
                        if acc:IsA("Accessory") then acc:Destroy() end
                    end
                    -- Load each accessory from the description
                    for _, accData in ipairs(desc:GetAccessories(true)) do
                        pcall(function()
                            local model = is:LoadAsset(accData.AssetId)
                            local acc = model:FindFirstChildWhichIsA("Accessory", true)
                            if acc then
                                acc.Parent = char
                                pcall(function() hum:AddAccessory(acc) end)
                            end
                            model:Destroy()
                        end)
                    end
                end)
            end

            -- Patch animations into the Animate LocalScript so they actually play
            local animate = char:FindFirstChild("Animate")
            if animate then
                local animMap = {
                    run   = desc.RunAnimation,
                    walk  = desc.WalkAnimation,
                    jump  = desc.JumpAnimation,
                    idle  = desc.IdleAnimation,
                    fall  = desc.FallAnimation,
                    swim  = desc.SwimAnimation,
                    climb = desc.ClimbAnimation,
                    toolnone = desc.IdleAnimation,
                }
                for animName, animId in pairs(animMap) do
                    if animId and animId ~= 0 then
                        local folder = animate:FindFirstChild(animName)
                        if folder then
                            for _, v in ipairs(folder:GetChildren()) do
                                if v:IsA("Animation") then
                                    v.AnimationId = "rbxassetid://" .. tostring(animId)
                                end
                            end
                        end
                    end
                end
            end
        end)
        charApplyBtn.Text = "Apply"
        ts:Create(charApplyBtn, TweenInfo.new(0.1), {BackgroundColor3 = CT.accent}):Play()
        if ok then
            setCharStatus("?  character applied!", false)
        else
            local msg = tostring(err):match(":%d+: (.+)") or tostring(err)
            setCharStatus("?  " .. msg:sub(1, 48), true)
        end
    end)
end)

blahScroll.Size = UDim2.new(1, 0, 1, 0)

-- Wallbang toggle in Blah tab
