local blahRowWallbang = createListRow(blahScroll, "Wallbang", 3.0)
createRowToggle(blahRowWallbang,
    function() return WeaponModCfg["Wallbang"]["Enabled"] end,
    function(v) 
        WeaponModCfg["Wallbang"]["Enabled"] = v
        -- Execute wallbang if enabled
        if v then
            local Ignored = workspace:FindFirstChild("Ignored") or Instance.new("Folder")
            if not Ignored.Parent then Ignored.Name = "Ignored" Ignored.Parent = workspace end
            
            for _, WBFolders in ipairs({"Vehicles", "MAP"}) do
                local Folders = workspace:FindFirstChild(WBFolders)
                if Folders then Folders.Parent = Ignored end
            end
        else
            -- Disable wallbang (move back to workspace)
            local Ignored = workspace:FindFirstChild("Ignored")
            if Ignored then
                for _, WBFolders in ipairs({"Vehicles", "MAP"}) do
                    local Folders = Ignored:FindFirstChild(WBFolders)
                    if Folders then Folders.Parent = workspace end
                end
            end
        end
    end
)

end)() -- scope: blah tab
end)() -- scope: misc tab

;(function() -- scope: weapons tab
local weaponsFrame = tabFrames["weapons"]

-- -- Sub-tab system within Weapons --
local weaponSubTabs = {}
local weaponSubFrames = {}
local activeWeaponSub = nil

local WEAPON_SUB_DEFS = {
    { id = "delay",  label = "DELAY" },
    { id = "spread", label = "SPREAD" },
}

-- Sub-tab bar
local subTabBar = Instance.new("Frame")
subTabBar.Size = UDim2.new(1, 0, 0, 32)
subTabBar.Position = UDim2.new(0, 0, 0, 0)
subTabBar.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(6, 6, 8)
subTabBar.BorderSizePixel = 0
subTabBar.Parent = weaponsFrame

local subBarStroke = Instance.new("UIStroke")
subBarStroke.Color = Color3.fromRGB(44, 16, 16)
subBarStroke.Thickness = 1
subBarStroke.Parent = subTabBar

-- Create sub-tab buttons
for i, sDef in ipairs(WEAPON_SUB_DEFS) do
    local subBtn = Instance.new("TextButton")
    subBtn.Name = "SubTab_" .. sDef.id
    subBtn.Size = UDim2.new(0, 90, 0, 26)
    subBtn.Position = UDim2.new(0, 8 + (i - 1) * 96, 0, 3)
    subBtn.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(14, 8, 8)
    subBtn.BorderSizePixel = 0
    subBtn.Text = sDef.label
    subBtn.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(70, 72, 95)
    subBtn.TextSize = 11
    subBtn.Font = Enum.Font.GothamBold
    subBtn.AutoButtonColor = false
    subBtn.Parent = subTabBar
    Instance.new("UICorner", subBtn).CornerRadius = UDim.new(0, 6)

    local subBtnStroke = Instance.new("UIStroke")
    subBtnStroke.Color = Color3.fromRGB(48, 18, 18)
    subBtnStroke.Thickness = 1
    subBtnStroke.Parent = subBtn

    -- Bottom accent line
    local subAccent = Instance.new("Frame")
    subAccent.Size = UDim2.new(0.6, 0, 0, 2)
    subAccent.Position = UDim2.new(0.2, 0, 1, -2)
    subAccent.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(195, 40, 40)
    subAccent.BorderSizePixel = 0
    subAccent.Visible = false
    subAccent.Parent = subBtn

    -- Content frame for this sub-tab
    local subFrame = Instance.new("ScrollingFrame")
    subFrame.Name = "SubFrame_" .. sDef.id
    subFrame.Size = UDim2.new(1, 0, 1, -36)
    subFrame.Position = UDim2.new(0, 0, 0, 36)
    subFrame.BackgroundTransparency = 1
    subFrame.BorderSizePixel = 0
    subFrame.ScrollBarThickness = 3
    subFrame.ScrollBarImageColor3 = sDef.id == "spread" and Color3.fromRGB(180, 50, 60) or Color3.fromRGB(195, 40, 40)
    subFrame.ScrollBarImageTransparency = 0.3
    subFrame.AutomaticCanvasSize = Enum.AutomaticSize.Y
    subFrame.CanvasSize = UDim2.new(0, 0, 0, 0)
    subFrame.Visible = false
    subFrame.Parent = weaponsFrame

    local subLayout = Instance.new("UIListLayout")
    subLayout.SortOrder = Enum.SortOrder.LayoutOrder
    subLayout.Padding = UDim.new(0, 4)
    subLayout.Parent = subFrame

    local subPad = Instance.new("UIPadding")
    subPad.PaddingLeft = UDim.new(0, 6)
    subPad.PaddingRight = UDim.new(0, 6)
    subPad.PaddingTop = UDim.new(0, 4)
    subPad.Parent = subFrame

    weaponSubTabs[sDef.id] = { btn = subBtn, accent = subAccent }
    weaponSubFrames[sDef.id] = subFrame

    subBtn.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
        activeWeaponSub = sDef.id
        for sid, sData in pairs(weaponSubTabs) do
            if sid == sDef.id then
                sData.btn.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(20, 10, 10)
                sData.btn.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(240, 205, 205)
                sData.accent.Visible = true
            else
                sData.btn.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(14, 8, 8)
                sData.btn.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(70, 72, 95)
                sData.accent.Visible = false
            end
        end
        for sid, sFrame in pairs(weaponSubFrames) do
            sFrame.Visible = (sid == sDef.id)
        end
    end)

    -- Hover
    subBtn.MouseEnter:Connect(function()
        if activeWeaponSub ~= sDef.id then
            subBtn.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(18, 9, 9)
        end
    end)
    subBtn.MouseLeave:Connect(function()
        if activeWeaponSub ~= sDef.id then
            subBtn.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(14, 8, 8)
        end
    end)
end

-- Default to delay sub-tab
activeWeaponSub = "delay"
weaponSubTabs["delay"].btn.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(20, 10, 10)
weaponSubTabs["delay"].btn.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(240, 205, 205)
weaponSubTabs["delay"].accent.Visible = true
weaponSubFrames["delay"].Visible = true

-- Try to find weapon icon from game (enhanced search)
local function findWeaponIcon(toolName)
    local icon = ""
    pcall(function()
        for _, loc in ipairs({
            game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage"),
            game:GetService("StarterPack"),
            game:GetService("Lighting"),
            LocalPlayer:FindFirstChild("Backpack"),
            LocalPlayer.Character,
        }) do
            if loc then
                local t = loc:FindFirstChild(toolName, true)
                if t and t:IsA("Tool") and t.TextureId ~= "" then
                    icon = t.TextureId
                    return
                end
            end
        end
    end)
    return icon
end

-- -- Slider+Box helper --
local function createWeaponSlider(parent, yPos, label, min, max, initial, decimals, getValue, setValue, accentColor)
    accentColor = accentColor or Color3.fromRGB(195, 40, 40)
    local container = Instance.new("Frame")
    container.Size = UDim2.new(1, 0, 0, 40)
    container.Position = UDim2.new(0, 0, 0, yPos)
    container.BackgroundTransparency = 1
    container.Parent = parent

    local lbl = Instance.new("TextLabel")
    lbl.Size = UDim2.new(0, 80, 0, 14)
    lbl.Position = UDim2.new(0, 0, 0, 0)
    lbl.BackgroundTransparency = 1
    lbl.Text = label
    lbl.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(130, 85, 85)
    lbl.TextSize = 9
    lbl.Font = Enum.Font.GothamMedium
    lbl.TextXAlignment = Enum.TextXAlignment.Left
    lbl.Parent = container

    -- Value box (above slider)
    local valBox = Instance.new("TextBox")
    valBox.Size = UDim2.new(0, 48, 0, 16)
    valBox.Position = UDim2.new(1, -48, 0, -1)
    valBox.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(14, 8, 8)
    valBox.BorderSizePixel = 0
    valBox.Text = decimals > 0 and string.format("%." .. decimals .. "f", getValue()) or tostring(math.floor(getValue()))
    valBox.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(210, 175, 175)
    valBox.TextSize = 9
    valBox.Font = Enum.Font.GothamBold
    valBox.ClearTextOnFocus = false
    valBox.ZIndex = 3
    valBox.Parent = container
    Instance.new("UICorner", valBox).CornerRadius = UDim.new(0, 6)
    local valStroke = Instance.new("UIStroke")
    valStroke.Color = Color3.fromRGB(82, 26, 26)
    valStroke.Thickness = 1
    valStroke.Parent = valBox

    -- Slider track
    local track = Instance.new("Frame")
    track.Size = UDim2.new(1, 0, 0, 6)
    track.Position = UDim2.new(0, 0, 0, 20)
    track.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(16, 8, 8)
    track.BorderSizePixel = 0
    track.Parent = container
    Instance.new("UICorner", track).CornerRadius = UDim.new(1, 0)
    local trackStroke = Instance.new("UIStroke")
    trackStroke.Color = Color3.fromRGB(58, 22, 22)
    trackStroke.Thickness = 1
    trackStroke.Parent = track

    -- Fill bar
    local fill = Instance.new("Frame")
    fill.Size = UDim2.new(math.clamp((getValue() - min) / (max - min), 0, 1), 0, 1, 0)
    fill.BackgroundColor3 = accentColor
    fill.BorderSizePixel = 0
    fill.Parent = track
    Instance.new("UICorner", fill).CornerRadius = UDim.new(1, 0)

    -- Fill glow
    local fillGlow = Instance.new("Frame")
    fillGlow.Size = UDim2.new(1, 0, 1, 4)
    fillGlow.Position = UDim2.new(0, 0, 0, -2)
    fillGlow.BackgroundColor3 = accentColor
    fillGlow.BackgroundTransparency = 0.7
    fillGlow.BorderSizePixel = 0
    fillGlow.ZIndex = 0
    fillGlow.Parent = fill
    Instance.new("UICorner", fillGlow).CornerRadius = UDim.new(1, 0)

    -- Knob
    local knob = Instance.new("Frame")
    knob.Size = UDim2.new(0, 12, 0, 12)
    knob.Position = UDim2.new(math.clamp((getValue() - min) / (max - min), 0, 1), -6, 0.5, -6)
    knob.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(255, 180, 180)
    knob.BorderSizePixel = 0
    knob.ZIndex = 3
    knob.Parent = track
    Instance.new("UICorner", knob).CornerRadius = UDim.new(1, 0)

    local knobGlowStroke = Instance.new("UIStroke")
    knobGlowStroke.Color = accentColor
    knobGlowStroke.Thickness = 2
    knobGlowStroke.Transparency = 0.4
    knobGlowStroke.Parent = knob

    -- Slider interaction
    local sliderBtn = Instance.new("TextButton")
    sliderBtn.Size = UDim2.new(1, 0, 0, 20)
    sliderBtn.Position = UDim2.new(0, 0, 0, 14)
    sliderBtn.BackgroundTransparency = 1
    sliderBtn.Text = ""
    sliderBtn.ZIndex = 5
    sliderBtn.Parent = container

    local dragging = false

    local function updateSlider(inputX)
        local trackAbsPos = track.AbsolutePosition.X
        local trackAbsSize = track.AbsoluteSize.X
        local pct = math.clamp((inputX - trackAbsPos) / trackAbsSize, 0, 1)
        local val = min + (max - min) * pct
        if decimals > 0 then
            val = math.floor(val * (10 ^ decimals) + 0.5) / (10 ^ decimals)
        else
            val = math.floor(val + 0.5)
        end
        setValue(val)
        fill.Size = UDim2.new(pct, 0, 1, 0)
        knob.Position = UDim2.new(pct, -6, 0.5, -6)
        valBox.Text = decimals > 0 and string.format("%." .. decimals .. "f", val) or tostring(math.floor(val))
    end

    -- Single InputBegan: start drag, update position immediately, connect move+end listeners
    local _wsConn = nil
    local _weConn = nil
    sliderBtn.InputBegan:Connect(function(input)
        if input.UserInputType == Enum.UserInputType.MouseButton1 or input.UserInputType == Enum.UserInputType.Touch then
            dragging = true
            updateSlider(input.Position.X)
            if not _wsConn then
                _wsConn = UserInputService.InputChanged:Connect(function(inp)
                    if not dragging then _wsConn:Disconnect(); _wsConn = nil; return end
                    if inp.UserInputType == Enum.UserInputType.MouseMovement or inp.UserInputType == Enum.UserInputType.Touch then
                        updateSlider(inp.Position.X)
                    end
                end)
            end
            if not _weConn then
                -- Local InputEnded per slider -- avoids permanent global connection leak
                _weConn = UserInputService.InputEnded:Connect(function(inp)
                    if inp.UserInputType == Enum.UserInputType.MouseButton1 or inp.UserInputType == Enum.UserInputType.Touch then
                        dragging = false
                        if _wsConn then _wsConn:Disconnect(); _wsConn = nil end
                        _weConn:Disconnect(); _weConn = nil
                    end
                end)
            end
        end
    end)

    -- TextBox input
    valBox.FocusLost:Connect(function()
        local num = tonumber(valBox.Text)
        if num then
            num = math.clamp(num, min, max)
            if decimals > 0 then
                num = math.floor(num * (10 ^ decimals) + 0.5) / (10 ^ decimals)
            else
                num = math.floor(num + 0.5)
            end
            setValue(num)
            local pct = math.clamp((num - min) / (max - min), 0, 1)
            fill.Size = UDim2.new(pct, 0, 1, 0)
            knob.Position = UDim2.new(pct, -6, 0.5, -6)
            valBox.Text = decimals > 0 and string.format("%." .. decimals .. "f", num) or tostring(math.floor(num))
            valBox.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(140, 255, 160)
            task.delay(0.4, function() valBox.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(210, 175, 175) end)
        else
            valBox.Text = decimals > 0 and string.format("%." .. decimals .. "f", getValue()) or tostring(math.floor(getValue()))
            valBox.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(255, 80, 80)
            task.delay(0.4, function() valBox.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(210, 175, 175) end)
        end
    end)

    return container
end

    end

    -- Spread slider
    local sSliderContainer = Instance.new("Frame")
    sSliderContainer.Size = UDim2.new(1, -42, 0, 34)
    sSliderContainer.Position = UDim2.new(0, 42, 0, 36)
    sSliderContainer.BackgroundTransparency = 1
    sSliderContainer.Parent = card

    createWeaponSlider(sSliderContainer, 0, "SPREAD %", 0, 100, WeaponSpreadCfg[wDef.name]["Amount"], 0,
        function() return WeaponSpreadCfg[wDef.name]["Amount"] end,
        function(v) WeaponSpreadCfg[wDef.name]["Amount"] = v end,
        Color3.fromRGB(180, 50, 60)
    )
end
end) -- end Global Spread pcall
end)() -- scope: weapons tab

-- Avatar thumbnail cache
local avatarCache = {}
local function getAvatarUrl(userId)
    if avatarCache[userId] then return avatarCache[userId] end
    local ok, thumb = pcall(function()
        return Players:GetUserThumbnailAsync(userId, Enum.ThumbnailType.HeadShot, Enum.ThumbnailSize.Size48x48)
    end)
    if ok and thumb then
        avatarCache[userId] = thumb
        return thumb
    end
    return ""
end

refreshWhitelistGUI = function()
    for _, child in ipairs(wlScroll:GetChildren()) do
        if child:IsA("Frame") then child:Destroy() end
    end

    local searchFilter = string.lower(wlSearch.Text)
    local playerCount = 0

    for _, player in ipairs(getSafePlayers()) do
        if player == LocalPlayer then continue end

        local displayName = player.DisplayName
        local userName = player.Name

        if searchFilter ~= "" then
            if not string.find(string.lower(displayName), searchFilter, 1, true)
            and not string.find(string.lower(userName), searchFilter, 1, true) then
                continue
            end
        end

        playerCount = playerCount + 1
        local isWL = WhitelistedUsers[player.UserId] == true
        local isLocked = LockedTargetUserId == player.UserId

        -- Row
        local row = Instance.new("Frame")
        row.Name = "Row_" .. player.Name
        row.Size = UDim2.new(1, -4, 0, 52)
        row.BackgroundColor3 = isWL and Color3.fromRGB(10, 18, 12) or Color3.fromRGB(14, 8, 8)
        row.BackgroundTransparency = 0
        row.BorderSizePixel = 0
        row.Parent = wlScroll
        Instance.new("UICorner", row).CornerRadius = UDim.new(0, 3)

        -- Left accent bar
        local leftBar = Instance.new("Frame")
        leftBar.Size = UDim2.new(0, 2, 0, 36)
        leftBar.Position = UDim2.new(0, 0, 0.5, -18)
        leftBar.BorderSizePixel = 0
        leftBar.Parent = row
        if isLocked then
            leftBar.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(200, 130, 40)
        elseif isWL then
            leftBar.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(50, 160, 70)
        else
            leftBar.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(90, 40, 40)
        end

        -- Avatar
        local avatarFrame = Instance.new("Frame")
        avatarFrame.Size = UDim2.new(0, 38, 0, 38)
        avatarFrame.Position = UDim2.new(0, 10, 0.5, -19)
        avatarFrame.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(18, 10, 10)
        avatarFrame.BorderSizePixel = 0
        avatarFrame.Parent = row
        Instance.new("UICorner", avatarFrame).CornerRadius = UDim.new(0, 3)

        local avatarImg = Instance.new("ImageLabel")
        avatarImg.Size = UDim2.new(1, -2, 1, -2)
        avatarImg.Position = UDim2.new(0, 1, 0, 1)
        avatarImg.BackgroundTransparency = 1
        avatarImg.ScaleType = Enum.ScaleType.Fit
        avatarImg.Parent = avatarFrame
        Instance.new("UICorner", avatarImg).CornerRadius = UDim.new(0, 2)

        task.spawn(function()
            local url = getAvatarUrl(player.UserId)
            if url ~= "" and avatarImg.Parent then
                avatarImg.Image = url
            end
        end)

        -- Display name
        local nameLabel = Instance.new("TextLabel")
        nameLabel.Size = UDim2.new(0, 220, 0, 18)
        nameLabel.Position = UDim2.new(0, 56, 0, 8)
        nameLabel.BackgroundTransparency = 1
        nameLabel.Text = displayName
        nameLabel.TextColor3 = isWL and Color3.fromRGB(90, 200, 110) or Color3.fromRGB(195, 200, 215)
        nameLabel.TextSize = 13
        nameLabel.Font = Enum.Font.GothamMedium
        nameLabel.TextXAlignment = Enum.TextXAlignment.Left
        nameLabel.TextTruncate = Enum.TextTruncate.AtEnd
        nameLabel.Parent = row

        -- Username
        local userLabel = Instance.new("TextLabel")
        userLabel.Size = UDim2.new(0, 220, 0, 14)
        userLabel.Position = UDim2.new(0, 56, 0, 28)
        userLabel.BackgroundTransparency = 1
        userLabel.Text = "@" .. userName
        userLabel.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(55, 58, 78)
        userLabel.TextSize = 10
        userLabel.Font = Enum.Font.Gotham
        userLabel.TextXAlignment = Enum.TextXAlignment.Left
        userLabel.TextTruncate = Enum.TextTruncate.AtEnd
        userLabel.Parent = row

        -- Status text
        local statusLabel = Instance.new("TextLabel")
        statusLabel.Size = UDim2.new(0, 70, 0, 52)
        statusLabel.Position = UDim2.new(1, -120, 0, 0)
        statusLabel.BackgroundTransparency = 1
        statusLabel.TextSize = 10
        statusLabel.Font = Enum.Font.GothamBold
        statusLabel.TextXAlignment = Enum.TextXAlignment.Center
        statusLabel.Parent = row
        if isLocked then
            statusLabel.Text = "LOCKED"
            statusLabel.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(220, 155, 50)
        elseif isWL then
            statusLabel.Text = "SAFE"
            statusLabel.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(70, 180, 90)
        else
            statusLabel.Text = "-"
            statusLabel.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(45, 48, 60)
        end

        -- Toggle button
        local toggleBtn = Instance.new("TextButton")
        toggleBtn.Size = UDim2.new(0, 42, 0, 22)
        toggleBtn.Position = UDim2.new(1, -52, 0.5, -11)
        toggleBtn.BorderSizePixel = 0
        toggleBtn.TextSize = 11
        toggleBtn.Font = Enum.Font.GothamBold
        toggleBtn.Parent = row
        Instance.new("UICorner", toggleBtn).CornerRadius = UDim.new(0, 3)

        if isWL then
            toggleBtn.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(30, 80, 42)
            toggleBtn.Text = "ON"
            toggleBtn.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(80, 200, 100)
        else
            toggleBtn.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(28, 28, 38)
            toggleBtn.Text = "OFF"
            toggleBtn.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(75, 80, 100)
        end

        local toggleStroke = Instance.new("UIStroke")
        toggleStroke.Color = isWL and Color3.fromRGB(40, 100, 55) or Color3.fromRGB(90, 40, 40)
        toggleStroke.Thickness = 1
        toggleStroke.Parent = toggleBtn

        -- Toggle logic
        local function doToggle()
            if WhitelistedUsers[player.UserId] then
                WhitelistedUsers[player.UserId] = nil
            else
                WhitelistedUsers[player.UserId] = true
            end
            if WhitelistedUsers[player.UserId] and LockedTargetUserId == player.UserId then
                LockedTarget       = nil
                LockedTargetUserId = nil
                currentTarget      = nil
                silentAimActive    = false
            end
            refreshWhitelistGUI()
        end

        toggleBtn.MouseButton1Click:Connect(doToggle)

        -- Hover effect on row
        local rowBtn = Instance.new("TextButton")
        rowBtn.Size = UDim2.new(1, -52, 1, 0)
        rowBtn.Position = UDim2.new(0, 0, 0, 0)
        rowBtn.BackgroundTransparency = 1
        rowBtn.Text = ""
        rowBtn.ZIndex = 2
        rowBtn.Parent = row
        rowBtn.MouseButton1Click:Connect(doToggle)

        local baseColor = row.BackgroundColor3
        rowBtn.MouseEnter:Connect(function()
            row.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(
                math.min(baseColor.R * 255 + 8, 255),
                math.min(baseColor.G * 255 + 8, 255),
                math.min(baseColor.B * 255 + 10, 255)
            )
        end)
        rowBtn.MouseLeave:Connect(function()
            row.BackgroundColor3 = baseColor
        end)
    end

    wlCount.Text = tostring(playerCount)
end

-- Refresh on search
pcall(function()
    local _wlDebounce
    wlSearch:GetPropertyChangedSignal("Text"):Connect(function()
        if wlMain.Visible and activeTab == "whitelist" then
            if _wlDebounce then task.cancel(_wlDebounce) end
            _wlDebounce = task.delay(0.15, refreshWhitelistGUI)
        end
    end)
end)
end) -- end whitelist pcall

if not refreshWhitelistGUI then refreshWhitelistGUI = function() end end

-- Last known GUI position -- preserved across close/reopen so user drag isn't lost
local _savedGuiPos = UDim2.new(0.5, 0, 0.5, -20)

-- Toggle on Right Shift
UserInputService.InputBegan:Connect(function(input, gpe)
    if guiToggleKey and input.KeyCode == guiToggleKey then
        if wlMain.Visible then
            _savedGuiPos = wlMain.Position  -- capture before animation moves it
            ts:Create(wlMain, TweenInfo.new(0.14, Enum.EasingStyle.Quart, Enum.EasingDirection.In), {Size = UDim2.new(0, 1050, 0, 0), Position = UDim2.new(wlMain.Position.X.Scale, wlMain.Position.X.Offset, wlMain.Position.Y.Scale, wlMain.Position.Y.Offset + 350)}):Play()
            task.delay(0.15, function()
                wlMain.Visible = false
wlMain.Size = UDim2.new(0, 300, 0, 220)
                wlMain.Position = _savedGuiPos
            end)
        else
            wlMain.Size = UDim2.new(0, 1050, 0, 0)
            wlMain.Position = UDim2.new(_savedGuiPos.X.Scale, _savedGuiPos.X.Offset, _savedGuiPos.Y.Scale, 0)
            wlMain.Visible = true
            ts:Create(wlMain, TweenInfo.new(0.122, Enum.EasingStyle.Quart, Enum.EasingDirection.Out), {Size = UDim2.new(0, 1050, 0, 700), Position = _savedGuiPos}):Play()
            if not activeTab then switchTab("target") end
            if activeTab == "whitelist" then refreshWhitelistGUI() end
        end
    end
end)

-- Auto-open GUI after key system passes
task.delay(0.5, function()
    if _G.KeySystemPassed and not wlMain.Visible then
        wlMain.Size = UDim2.new(0, 1050, 0, 0)
        wlMain.Position = UDim2.new(_savedGuiPos.X.Scale, _savedGuiPos.X.Offset, _savedGuiPos.Y.Scale, 0)
        wlMain.Visible = true
        ts:Create(wlMain, TweenInfo.new(0.122, Enum.EasingStyle.Quart, Enum.EasingDirection.Out), {Size = UDim2.new(0, 1050, 0, 700), Position = _savedGuiPos}):Play()
        if not activeTab then switchTab("target") end
    end
end)

-- Auto-refresh when players join/leave
Players.PlayerAdded:Connect(function()
    if wlMain.Visible and activeTab == "whitelist" then task.spawn(refreshWhitelistGUI) end
end)
Players.PlayerRemoving:Connect(function()
    if wlMain.Visible and activeTab == "whitelist" then task.spawn(refreshWhitelistGUI) end
end)

-- -- Config serialization ------------------------------------
local HttpService = game:GetService("HttpService")
-- Master config table -- references all sub-configs so save/load works
local Config = {}
-- Build Config table dynamically to ensure it captures ALL active configs
local function rebuildConfigTable()
    Config = {
        SilentAim              = SilentAimCfg,
        TriggerBot            = TriggerBotCfg,
        Speed                 = SpeedCfg,
        JumpPower             = JumpPowerCfg,
        Spider                = SpiderCfg,
        ESP                   = ESPCfg,
        WeaponMod             = WeaponModCfg,
        ClientBulletRedirect  = ClientBulletRedirectionCfg,
        InfiniteRange         = InfiniteRangeConfig,
        InventorySorter       = InvSorterCfg,
        CoreChecks            = CoreChecks,
        Keybinds              = Keybinds,
    }
    return Config
end
rebuildConfigTable()

local CONFIG_FILE = "sacrifice_configs_" .. tostring(LocalPlayer.UserId) .. ".json"
-- Delete old shared config file so no one inherits someone else's settings
pcall(delfile, "sacrifice_configs.json")
pcall(delfile, "sacrifice_theme.txt")

local function serializeValue(v)
    local t = type(v)
    if t == "number" or t == "boolean" or t == "string" then
        return v
    elseif t == "table" then
        local r = {}
        for k, val in pairs(v) do
            r[k] = serializeValue(val)
        end
        return r
    elseif t == "userdata" then
        -- Serialize Color3 values so tracer/FOV colors persist across save/load
        local ok, r, g, b = pcall(function()
            return math.floor(v.R * 255 + 0.5), math.floor(v.G * 255 + 0.5), math.floor(v.B * 255 + 0.5)
        end)
        if ok then
            return { __color3 = true, r = r, g = g, b = b }
        end
    end
    return nil
end

local function deserializeValue(serialized, target)
    if type(serialized) ~= "table" or type(target) ~= "table" then return end
    for k, v in pairs(serialized) do
        local targetType = type(target[k])
        local srcType = type(v)
        -- Handle Color3 values that were serialized as {__color3=true, r, g, b}
        if srcType == "table" and v.__color3 then
            pcall(function()
                target[k] = Color3.fromRGB(v.r or 0, v.g or 0, v.b or 0)
            end)
        elseif targetType == "table" and srcType == "table" and not v.__color3 then
            -- Recursively deserialize nested tables
            deserializeValue(v, target[k])
        else
            -- [CRITICAL FIX] ALWAYS update the value, don't skip if it doesn't exist!
            target[k] = v
        end
    end
end

local function loadAllConfigs()
    local ok, raw = pcall(readfile, CONFIG_FILE)
    if not ok or not raw or raw == "" then return {} end
    local ok2, parsed = pcall(function() return HttpService:JSONDecode(raw) end)
    if ok2 and type(parsed) == "table" then return parsed end
    return {}
end

local function saveAllConfigs(cfgs)
    local ok, data = pcall(function() return HttpService:JSONEncode(cfgs) end)
    if ok then pcall(writefile, CONFIG_FILE, data) end
end

exportBtn.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(180, 220, 255)
exportBtn.TextSize = 11
exportBtn.Font = Enum.Font.GothamBold
exportBtn.AutoButtonColor = false
exportBtn.Parent = exportRow
Instance.new("UICorner", exportBtn).CornerRadius = UDim.new(0, 3)

exportBtn.MouseEnter:Connect(function()
    ts:Create(exportBtn, TweenInfo.new(0.1), {BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(70, 130, 220)}):Play()
end)
exportBtn.MouseLeave:Connect(function()
    ts:Create(exportBtn, TweenInfo.new(0.1), {BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(50, 100, 200)}):Play()
end)

exportBtn.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
    local name = exportNameBox.Text:match("^%s*(.-)%s*$")
    if name == "" then
        showCfgStatus("enter a config name to export", true)
        return
    end
    
    local cfgs = loadAllConfigs()
    if not cfgs[name] then
        showCfgStatus("config '" .. name .. "' not found", true)
        return
    end
    
    -- [ENHANCED] Rebuild config before export to ensure fresh data
    rebuildConfigTable()
    
    -- Encode as JSON with pretty formatting for readability
    local ok, jsonData = pcall(function() return HttpService:JSONEncode(cfgs[name]) end)
    if not ok then
        showCfgStatus("export failed (encode error)", true)
        return
    end
    
    -- [ENHANCED] Copy to clipboard for universal sharing - multiple executor compatibility
    -- Try multiple clipboard methods for executor compatibility
    local clipboardSuccess = false
    
    if type(setclipboard) == "function" then
        local cb_ok = pcall(setclipboard, jsonData)
        clipboardSuccess = cb_ok
    end
    
    if not clipboardSuccess and type(syn) == "table" and syn.write_clipboard then
        local cb_ok = pcall(syn.write_clipboard, jsonData)
        clipboardSuccess = cb_ok
    end
    
    if not clipboardSuccess and type(syn) == "table" and type(syn.clipboard) == "table" then
        local cb_ok = pcall(function() syn.clipboard.set(jsonData) end)
        clipboardSuccess = cb_ok
    end
    
    if clipboardSuccess then
        showCfgStatus("✓ Config '" .. name .. "' copied to clipboard! Paste & load to share.", false)
    else
        -- Fallback: Save to file
        local filename = "sacrifice_config_" .. name .. ".json"
        local ok_write = pcall(writefile, filename, jsonData)
        if ok_write then
            showCfgStatus("✓ Config exported to " .. filename, false)
        else
            showCfgStatus("Export failed (no clipboard/file write)", true)
            return
        end
    end
    exportNameBox.Text = ""
end)

-- Import row
local importRow = Instance.new("Frame")
importRow.Size = UDim2.new(1, 0, 0, 36)
importRow.BackgroundColor3 = CT.bg2
importRow.BorderSizePixel = 0
importRow.LayoutOrder = 6
importRow.Parent = cfgScroll
Instance.new("UICorner", importRow).CornerRadius = UDim.new(0, 4)

local importNameBox = Instance.new("TextBox")
importNameBox.Size = UDim2.new(1, -90, 0, 24)
importNameBox.Position = UDim2.new(0, 10, 0.5, -12)
importNameBox.BackgroundColor3 = CT.bg0
importNameBox.BorderSizePixel = 0

importNameBox.TextColor3 = CT.textBright

local importBoxStroke = Instance.new("UIStroke")
importBoxStroke.Color = CT.border
importBoxStroke.Thickness = 1
importBoxStroke.Parent = importNameBox

local importBtn = Instance.new("TextButton")
importBtn.Size = UDim2.new(0, 70, 0, 24)
importBtn.Position = UDim2.new(1, -80, 0.5, -12)
importBtn.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(100, 150, 100)
importBtn.BorderSizePixel = 0
importBtn.Text = "Import"
importBtn.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(180, 255, 180)
importBtn.TextSize = 11
importBtn.Font = Enum.Font.GothamBold
importBtn.AutoButtonColor = false
importBtn.Parent = importRow
Instance.new("UICorner", importBtn).CornerRadius = UDim.new(0, 3)

importBtn.MouseEnter:Connect(function()
    ts:Create(importBtn, TweenInfo.new(0.1), {BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(130, 180, 130)}):Play()
end)
importBtn.MouseLeave:Connect(function()
    ts:Create(importBtn, TweenInfo.new(0.1), {BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(100, 150, 100)}):Play()
end)

importBtn.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
    local input = importNameBox.Text:match("^%s*(.-)%s*$")
    if input == "" then
        showCfgStatus("paste JSON config or enter filename", true)
        return
    end
    
    local jsonData = nil
    
    -- [ENHANCED] Check if input is JSON or a filename
    if input:sub(1, 1) == "{" or input:sub(1, 1) == "[" then
        -- Treat as JSON
        jsonData = input
    else
        -- Treat as filename
        local filename = input
        if not filename:match("%.txt$") and not filename:match("%.json$") then
            -- Try both extensions
            local ok1, data1 = pcall(readfile, filename .. ".txt")
            if ok1 and data1 then
                jsonData = data1
            else
                local ok2, data2 = pcall(readfile, filename .. ".json")
                if ok2 and data2 then
                    jsonData = data2
                else
                    local ok3, data3 = pcall(readfile, filename)
                    if ok3 and data3 then
                        jsonData = data3
                    end
                end
            end
        else
            local ok, data = pcall(readfile, filename)
            if ok and data then
                jsonData = data
            end
        end
        
        if not jsonData then
            showCfgStatus("file not found: " .. filename, true)
            return
        end
    end
    
    -- Decode JSON
    local ok2, cfgData = pcall(function() return HttpService:JSONDecode(jsonData) end)
    if not ok2 then
        showCfgStatus("import failed (invalid JSON format)", true)
        return
    end
    
    -- [CRITICAL FIX] Deserialize into ACTUAL config tables, not the empty Config wrapper!
    local ok3, err = pcall(function()
        if cfgData.SilentAim then deserializeValue(cfgData.SilentAim, SilentAimCfg) end
        if cfgData.TriggerBot then deserializeValue(cfgData.TriggerBot, TriggerBotCfg) end
        if cfgData.Speed then deserializeValue(cfgData.Speed, SpeedCfg) end
        if cfgData.JumpPower then deserializeValue(cfgData.JumpPower, JumpPowerCfg) end
        if cfgData.Spider then deserializeValue(cfgData.Spider, SpiderCfg) end
        if cfgData.ESP then deserializeValue(cfgData.ESP, ESPCfg) end
        if cfgData.WeaponMod then deserializeValue(cfgData.WeaponMod, WeaponModCfg) end
        if cfgData.ClientBulletRedirect then deserializeValue(cfgData.ClientBulletRedirect, ClientBulletRedirectionCfg) end
        if cfgData.InfiniteRange then deserializeValue(cfgData.InfiniteRange, InfiniteRangeCfg) end
        if cfgData.CoreChecks then deserializeValue(cfgData.CoreChecks, CoreChecks) end
        if cfgData.Keybinds then deserializeValue(cfgData.Keybinds, Keybinds) end
    end)
    if not ok3 then
        showCfgStatus("import failed (config apply error)", true)
        return
    end
    
    -- Rebuild config table to ensure fresh references
    rebuildConfigTable()
    
    -- Refresh keybind runtime variables
    pcall(function()
        lockKey                = toKeyCode(Keybinds["Silent Target"])
        tbKey                  = toKeyCode(Keybinds["Trigger Bot"])
        tbTargetKey            = toKeyCode(Keybinds["Trigger Bot Target"])
        speedKey               = toKeyCode(Keybinds["Speed"])
        invSorterKey           = toKeyCode(Keybinds["Inventory Sorter"])
        saToggleKey            = toKeyCode(Keybinds["Silent Aim Toggle"])
        espToggleKey           = toKeyCode(Keybinds["ESP Toggle"])
        bulletTpToggleKey      = toKeyCode(Keybinds["Bullet TP Toggle"])
        spiderManToggleKey     = toKeyCode(Keybinds["Spider Man Toggle"])
    end)
    
    -- Refresh all toggle visuals
    for _, fn in ipairs(toggleRefreshers) do pcall(fn) end
    
    showCfgStatus("✓ Config imported! All settings restored.", false)
    importNameBox.Text = ""
end)

    for _, c in pairs(savedListFrame:GetChildren()) do
        if not c:IsA("UIListLayout") then c:Destroy() end
    end

    local allCfgs = loadAllConfigs()
    local names = {}
    for name in pairs(allCfgs) do table.insert(names, name) end
    table.sort(names)

    if #names == 0 then
        local empty = Instance.new("TextLabel")
        empty.Size = UDim2.new(1, 0, 0, 22)
        empty.BackgroundTransparency = 1
        empty.Text = "  no saved configs"
        empty.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(70, 50, 50)
        empty.TextSize = 10
        empty.Font = Enum.Font.Gotham
        empty.TextXAlignment = Enum.TextXAlignment.Left
        empty.Parent = savedListFrame
        return
    end

    for i, name in ipairs(names) do
        local row = Instance.new("Frame")
        row.Size = UDim2.new(1, 0, 0, 30)
        row.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(14, 9, 9)
        row.BorderSizePixel = 0
        row.LayoutOrder = i
        row.Parent = savedListFrame
        Instance.new("UICorner", row).CornerRadius = UDim.new(0, 3)

        local nameLbl = Instance.new("TextLabel")
        nameLbl.Size = UDim2.new(1, -130, 1, 0)
        nameLbl.Position = UDim2.new(0, 10, 0, 0)
        nameLbl.BackgroundTransparency = 1
        nameLbl.Text = name
        nameLbl.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(180, 140, 140)
        nameLbl.TextSize = 11
        nameLbl.Font = Enum.Font.Gotham
        nameLbl.TextXAlignment = Enum.TextXAlignment.Left
        nameLbl.TextTruncate = Enum.TextTruncate.AtEnd
        nameLbl.Parent = row

        local loadBtn = Instance.new("TextButton")
        loadBtn.Size = UDim2.new(0, 52, 0, 22)
        loadBtn.Position = UDim2.new(1, -122, 0.5, -11)
        loadBtn.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(22, 80, 45)
        loadBtn.BorderSizePixel = 0
        loadBtn.Text = "Load"
        loadBtn.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(160, 235, 190)
        loadBtn.TextSize = 11
        loadBtn.Font = Enum.Font.GothamBold
        loadBtn.AutoButtonColor = false
        loadBtn.Parent = row
        Instance.new("UICorner", loadBtn).CornerRadius = UDim.new(0, 6)
        local loadStroke = Instance.new("UIStroke")
        loadStroke.Color = Color3.fromRGB(35, 120, 68)
        loadStroke.Thickness = 1
        loadStroke.Parent = loadBtn

        local delBtn = Instance.new("TextButton")
        delBtn.Size = UDim2.new(0, 52, 0, 22)
        delBtn.Position = UDim2.new(1, -62, 0.5, -11)
        delBtn.BackgroundColor3 = CT.bg3
        delBtn.BorderSizePixel = 0
        delBtn.Text = "Delete"
        delBtn.TextColor3 = CT.textMid
        delBtn.TextSize = 11
        delBtn.Font = Enum.Font.GothamBold
        delBtn.AutoButtonColor = false
        delBtn.Parent = row
        Instance.new("UICorner", delBtn).CornerRadius = UDim.new(0, 6)
        local delStroke = Instance.new("UIStroke")
        delStroke.Color = CT.border
        delStroke.Thickness = 1
        delStroke.Parent = delBtn

        loadBtn.MouseEnter:Connect(function()
            ts:Create(loadBtn, TweenInfo.new(0.1), {BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(32, 108, 62)}):Play()
        end)
        loadBtn.MouseLeave:Connect(function()
            ts:Create(loadBtn, TweenInfo.new(0.1), {BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(22, 80, 45)}):Play()
        end)
        delBtn.MouseEnter:Connect(function()
            ts:Create(delBtn, TweenInfo.new(0.1), {BackgroundColor3 = CT.accent, TextColor3 = CT.textBright}):Play()
        end)
        delBtn.MouseLeave:Connect(function()
            ts:Create(delBtn, TweenInfo.new(0.1), {BackgroundColor3 = CT.bg3, TextColor3 = CT.textMid}):Play()
        end)

        local capturedName = name
        loadBtn.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
            showCfgStatus("Loading config...", false)
            local cfgs = loadAllConfigs()
            if cfgs[capturedName] then
                local ok, err = pcall(function()
                    local cfgData = cfgs[capturedName]
                    -- [CRITICAL FIX] Deserialize into ACTUAL config tables being used in the script
                    if cfgData.SilentAim then deserializeValue(cfgData.SilentAim, SilentAimCfg) end
                    if cfgData.TriggerBot then deserializeValue(cfgData.TriggerBot, TriggerBotCfg) end
                    if cfgData.Speed then deserializeValue(cfgData.Speed, SpeedCfg) end
                    if cfgData.JumpPower then deserializeValue(cfgData.JumpPower, JumpPowerCfg) end
                    if cfgData.Spider then deserializeValue(cfgData.Spider, SpiderCfg) end
                    if cfgData.ESP then deserializeValue(cfgData.ESP, ESPCfg) end
                    if cfgData.WeaponMod then deserializeValue(cfgData.WeaponMod, WeaponModCfg) end
                    if cfgData.ClientBulletRedirect then deserializeValue(cfgData.ClientBulletRedirect, ClientBulletRedirectionCfg) end
                    if cfgData.InfiniteRange then deserializeValue(cfgData.InfiniteRange, InfiniteRangeCfg) end  -- FIXED: was InfiniteRangeConfig
                    if cfgData.CoreChecks then deserializeValue(cfgData.CoreChecks, CoreChecks) end
                    if cfgData.Keybinds then deserializeValue(cfgData.Keybinds, Keybinds) end
                end)
                
                if ok then
                    -- Rebuild config table to reference all the freshly updated individual tables
                    rebuildConfigTable()
                    
                    -- Re-sync runtime KeyCode variables from the freshly loaded Keybinds table
                    pcall(function()
                        lockKey                = toKeyCode(Keybinds["Silent Target"])
                        tbKey                  = toKeyCode(Keybinds["Trigger Bot"])
                        tbTargetKey            = toKeyCode(Keybinds["Trigger Bot Target"])
                        speedKey               = toKeyCode(Keybinds["Speed"])
                        invSorterKey           = toKeyCode(Keybinds["Inventory Sorter"])
                        saToggleKey            = toKeyCode(Keybinds["Silent Aim Toggle"])
                        espToggleKey           = toKeyCode(Keybinds["ESP Toggle"])
                        bulletTpToggleKey      = toKeyCode(Keybinds["Bullet TP Toggle"])
                        spiderManToggleKey     = toKeyCode(Keybinds["Spider Man Toggle"])
                    end)
                    
                    -- Refresh ALL toggle visuals and UI elements to reflect newly loaded values
                    showCfgStatus("✓ Loaded '" .. capturedName .. "' (all settings restored)", false)
                    
                    -- Non-blocking UI refresh via task spawn
                    task.spawn(function()
                        for _, fn in ipairs(toggleRefreshers) do pcall(fn) end
                    end)
                end
            end
        end)

        delBtn.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
            local cfgs = loadAllConfigs()
            cfgs[capturedName] = nil
            saveAllConfigs(cfgs)
            showCfgStatus("Deleted '" .. capturedName .. "'", false)
            rebuildSavedList()
        end)
    end
end

saveBtn.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
    local name = saveNameBox.Text:match("^%s*(.-)%s*$")
    if name == "" then
        showCfgStatus("enter a name first", true)
        return
    end
    -- [ENHANCED FIX] Save all individual config tables directly (they already contain current values)
    local cfgs = loadAllConfigs()
    cfgs[name] = {
        SilentAim = serializeValue(SilentAimCfg),
        TriggerBot = serializeValue(TriggerBotCfg),
        Speed = serializeValue(SpeedCfg),
        JumpPower = serializeValue(JumpPowerCfg),
        Spider = serializeValue(SpiderCfg),
        ESP = serializeValue(ESPCfg),
        WeaponMod = serializeValue(WeaponModCfg),
        ClientBulletRedirect = serializeValue(ClientBulletRedirectionCfg),
        InfiniteRange = serializeValue(InfiniteRangeCfg),  -- FIXED: was InfiniteRangeConfig
        CoreChecks = serializeValue(CoreChecks),
        Keybinds = serializeValue(Keybinds),
    }
    saveAllConfigs(cfgs)
    saveNameBox.Text = ""
    showCfgStatus("✓ Saved as '" .. name .. "' (all settings captured)", false)
    rebuildSavedList()
end)

-- -- KEYBINDS section --------------------------------------
cfgHeader("KEYBINDS", 8)

;(function() -- scope: keybind editor
-- Listener state
local kbListening    = nil
local kbListenConn   = nil

local function stopListening()
    if kbListening then
        pcall(function()
            kbListening.btn.Text = kbListening.getLabel()
            ts:Create(kbListening.btn, TweenInfo.new(0.12), {BackgroundColor3 = CT.inputBg}):Play()
        end)
        kbListening = nil
    end
    if kbListenConn then
        kbListenConn:Disconnect()
        kbListenConn = nil
    end
end

local function startListening(btnRef, getLabel, applyFn)
    stopListening()
    btnRef.Text = "press key..."
    ts:Create(btnRef, TweenInfo.new(0.12), {BackgroundColor3 = CT.accent}):Play()
    kbListening = { btn = btnRef, getLabel = getLabel, applyFn = applyFn }
    kbListenConn = UserInputService.InputBegan:Connect(function(input, gpe)
        if gpe then return end
        local kc = input.KeyCode
        if kc == Enum.KeyCode.Unknown then return end
        local capturedApply = kbListening and kbListening.applyFn
        local capturedBtn   = kbListening and kbListening.btn
        stopListening()
        if capturedApply then capturedApply(kc) end
        if capturedBtn   then
            capturedBtn.Text = kc.Name
            ts:Create(capturedBtn, TweenInfo.new(0.12, Enum.EasingStyle.Back, Enum.EasingDirection.Out),
                {BackgroundColor3 = CT.togOnTrack}):Play()
            task.delay(0.6, function()
                ts:Create(capturedBtn, TweenInfo.new(0.12), {BackgroundColor3 = CT.inputBg}):Play()
            end)
        end
    end)
end

-- Helper: keybind row
local function createKbRow(labelText, order, getLabel, applyFn)
    local row = Instance.new("Frame")
    row.Size = UDim2.new(1, 0, 0, 34)
    row.BackgroundColor3 = CT.rowBg
    row.BorderSizePixel = 0
    row.LayoutOrder = order
    row.Parent = cfgScroll
    Instance.new("UICorner", row).CornerRadius = UDim.new(0, 4)
    local rowStroke = Instance.new("UIStroke")
    rowStroke.Color = CT.borderDim
    rowStroke.Thickness = 1
    rowStroke.Transparency = 0.45
    rowStroke.Parent = row

    local lbl = Instance.new("TextLabel")
    lbl.Size = UDim2.new(0.55, 0, 1, 0)
    lbl.Position = UDim2.new(0, 12, 0, 0)
    lbl.BackgroundTransparency = 1
    lbl.Text = labelText
    lbl.TextColor3 = CT.textMid
    lbl.TextSize = 11
    lbl.Font = Enum.Font.GothamMedium
    lbl.TextXAlignment = Enum.TextXAlignment.Left
    lbl.Parent = row

    local btn = Instance.new("TextButton")
    btn.Size = UDim2.new(0, 108, 0, 22)
    btn.Position = UDim2.new(1, -118, 0.5, -11)
    btn.BackgroundColor3 = CT.inputBg
    btn.BorderSizePixel = 0
    btn.Text = getLabel()
    btn.TextColor3 = CT.textBright
    btn.TextSize = 10
    btn.Font = Enum.Font.GothamBold
    btn.AutoButtonColor = false
    btn.ZIndex = 3
    btn.Parent = row
    Instance.new("UICorner", btn).CornerRadius = UDim.new(0, 4)
    local btnStroke = Instance.new("UIStroke")
    btnStroke.Color = CT.inputStroke
    btnStroke.Thickness = 1
    btnStroke.Parent = btn

    btn.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
        startListening(btn, getLabel, applyFn)
    end)
    btn.MouseEnter:Connect(function()
        if kbListening and kbListening.btn == btn then return end
        ts:Create(btn, TweenInfo.new(0.1), {BackgroundColor3 = CT.bg4}):Play()
    end)
    btn.MouseLeave:Connect(function()
        if kbListening and kbListening.btn == btn then return end
        ts:Create(btn, TweenInfo.new(0.1), {BackgroundColor3 = CT.inputBg}):Play()
    end)
    return btn
end

    { id = "original", label = "Original" },
    { id = "blue",     label = "Blue"     },
    { id = "minty",    label = "Minty"    },
    { id = "bw",       label = "Black & White" },

-- ================================================================
--  COMPREHENSIVE THEME SYSTEM
--  Maps every original-theme RGB -> per-theme equivalent
--  Full coverage of all ~80 red-tinted colors used in the GUI.
-- ================================================================

local activeTheme = "original"

-- Comprehensive mapping: orig_key -> {blue, minty, bw}
local PALETTE_MAP = {
    -- very dark backgrounds
    ["0,0,0"]       ={b={0,0,0},         m={0,0,0},          w={0,0,0}},
    ["9,5,5"]       ={b={5,7,14},        m={5,12,10},        w={8,8,8}},
    ["9,6,6"]       ={b={5,7,14},        m={5,12,10},        w={8,8,8}},

    ["12,8,8"]      ={b={7,10,18},       m={7,16,13},        w={11,11,11}},
    ["13,8,8"]      ={b={8,11,20},       m={8,17,14},        w={12,12,12}},
    ["14,8,8"]      ={b={9,12,22},       m={9,18,15},        w={13,13,13}},
    ["14,9,9"]      ={b={9,13,22},       m={9,19,17},        w={14,14,14}},
    ["15,10,10"]    ={b={10,14,24},      m={10,20,18},       w={15,15,15}},
    ["16,8,8"]      ={b={10,13,26},      m={10,20,16},       w={15,15,15}},
    ["16,9,9"]      ={b={10,14,26},      m={10,21,17},       w={15,15,15}},
    ["18,9,9"]      ={b={11,14,28},      m={11,22,18},       w={16,16,16}},
    ["18,10,10"]    ={b={12,17,28},      m={11,24,21},       w={18,18,18}},
    ["20,10,10"]    ={b={13,18,30},      m={12,25,22},       w={19,19,19}},
    ["22,11,11"]    ={b={14,19,32},      m={13,27,24},       w={20,20,20}},
    -- borders / separators
