-- Builds a lookup: "r,g,b" -> Color3 for a given themeId
local function buildLookup(themeId)
    local t = {}
    for k, v in pairs(PALETTE_MAP) do
        local entry
        if themeId == "blue" then
            entry = v.b
        elseif themeId == "minty" then
            entry = v.m
        elseif themeId == "bw" then
            if v.w then
                entry = v.w
            else
                -- Fallback: convert to perceived luminance for any unlisted color
                local r, g, b = k:match("(%d+),(%d+),(%d+)")
                r, g, b = tonumber(r), tonumber(g), tonumber(b)
                if r and g and b then
                    -- Perceived luminance (BT.601). Reds have low natural luminance,
                    -- so we boost: emphasize max channel so dark accents read as grey
                    local lum = math.floor(0.2126*r + 0.7152*g + 0.0722*b + 0.5)
                    -- Slightly stretch contrast
                    lum = math.clamp(math.floor(lum * 1.15 + 0.5), 0, 255)
                    t[k] = Color3.fromRGB(lum, lum, lum)
                end
            end
        end  -- original: no remapping needed
        if entry then
            t[k] = Color3.fromRGB(entry[1], entry[2], entry[3])
        end
    end
    return t
end

local function colorKey(r,g,b)
    return math.floor(r+0.5)..","..math.floor(g+0.5)..","..math.floor(b+0.5)
end

local function applyTheme(themeId)
    if not themeId then return end
    activeTheme = themeId

    -- 1. Update CT semantic table
    local newCT = THEME_CT[themeId]
    if newCT then
        for k, v in pairs(newCT) do CT[k] = v end
    end

    -- 2. Persist preference
    pcall(writefile, "sacrifice_theme_" .. tostring(LocalPlayer.UserId) .. ".txt", themeId)

    -- 3. Walk GUI descendants and remap colors (OPTIMIZED)
    if themeId ~= "original" then
        task.spawn(function()
            local lookup = buildLookup(themeId)
            local descendants = wlMain:GetDescendants()
            
            for _, inst in ipairs(descendants) do
                pcall(function()
                    if inst.BackgroundTransparency < 1 then
                        local c = inst.BackgroundColor3
                        local k = colorKey(c.R*255, c.G*255, c.B*255)
                        if lookup[k] then inst.BackgroundColor3 = lookup[k] end
                    end
                    
                    local c = inst.TextColor3
                    local k = colorKey(c.R*255, c.G*255, c.B*255)
                    if lookup[k] then inst.TextColor3 = lookup[k] end
                    
                    local c2 = inst.ImageColor3
                    local k2 = colorKey(c2.R*255, c2.G*255, c2.B*255)
                    if lookup[k2] then inst.ImageColor3 = lookup[k2] end
                end)
                
                if inst:IsA("UIStroke") then
                    pcall(function()
                        local c = inst.Color
                        local k = colorKey(c.R*255, c.G*255, c.B*255)
                        if lookup[k] then inst.Color = lookup[k] end
                    end)
                end
                
                if inst:IsA("ScrollingFrame") then
                    pcall(function()
                        local c = inst.ScrollBarImageColor3
                        local k = colorKey(c.R*255, c.G*255, c.B*255)
                        if lookup[k] then inst.ScrollBarImageColor3 = lookup[k] end
                    end)
                end
                
                pcall(function()
                    local c = inst.PlaceholderColor3
                    local k = colorKey(c.R*255, c.G*255, c.B*255)
                    if lookup[k] then inst.PlaceholderColor3 = lookup[k] end
                end)
            end
        end)
    else
        -- Revert to original
        task.spawn(function()
            local reverseMap = {}
            for _, tid in ipairs({"blue","minty","bw"}) do
                local theme = THEME_CT[tid]
                for ctKey, themeColor in pairs(theme) do
                    local origColor = THEME_CT.original[ctKey]
                    if origColor then
                        local tk = colorKey(themeColor.R*255, themeColor.G*255, themeColor.B*255)
                        if not reverseMap[tk] then reverseMap[tk] = origColor end
                    end
                end
            end
            
            local descendants = wlMain:GetDescendants()
            for _, inst in ipairs(descendants) do
                pcall(function()
                    if inst.BackgroundTransparency < 1 then
                        local c = inst.BackgroundColor3
                        local k = colorKey(c.R*255, c.G*255, c.B*255)
                        if reverseMap[k] then inst.BackgroundColor3 = reverseMap[k] end
                    end
                    
                    local c = inst.TextColor3
                    local k = colorKey(c.R*255, c.G*255, c.B*255)
                    if reverseMap[k] then inst.TextColor3 = reverseMap[k] end
                    
                    local c2 = inst.ImageColor3
                    local k2 = colorKey(c2.R*255, c2.G*255, c2.B*255)
                    if reverseMap[k2] then inst.ImageColor3 = reverseMap[k2] end
                end)
                
                if inst:IsA("UIStroke") then
                    pcall(function()
                        local c = inst.Color
                        local k = colorKey(c.R*255, c.G*255, c.B*255)
                        if reverseMap[k] then inst.Color = reverseMap[k] end
                    end)
                end
                
                if inst:IsA("ScrollingFrame") then
                    pcall(function()
                        local c = inst.ScrollBarImageColor3
                        local k = colorKey(c.R*255, c.G*255, c.B*255)
                        if reverseMap[k] then inst.ScrollBarImageColor3 = reverseMap[k] end
                    end)
                end
                
                pcall(function()
                    local c = inst.PlaceholderColor3
                    local k = colorKey(c.R*255, c.G*255, c.B*255)
                    if reverseMap[k] then inst.PlaceholderColor3 = reverseMap[k] end
                end)
            end
        end)
    end

    -- 4. Update UIGradients
    for _, entry in ipairs(namedGrads) do pcall(function() entry.grad.Color = entry.fn() end) end

    -- 5. Re-apply CT
    pcall(function() wlMain.BackgroundColor3 = CT.bg1 end)
    pcall(function() wlTopLine.BackgroundColor3 = CT.topLine end)
    pcall(function() wlBorderStroke.Color = CT.borderDim end)
    pcall(function() wlTitleBar.BackgroundColor3 = CT.bg2 end)
    pcall(function() sidebar.BackgroundColor3 = CT.bg0 end)
    pcall(function() sidebarSep.BackgroundColor3 = CT.borderDim end)
    pcall(function() wlSep1.BackgroundColor3 = CT.border end)
    pcall(function() wlClose.BackgroundColor3 = CT.closeNorm end)
    pcall(function() wlClose.TextColor3 = CT.closeIcon end)
    pcall(function() wlCloseStroke.Color = CT.accent end)
    pcall(function() capyLogo.ImageColor3 = CT.textBright end)

    -- 6. Refresh toggle states
    for _, fn in ipairs(toggleRefreshers) do pcall(fn) end

    -- 7. Re-apply tab active state
    switchTab(activeTab)
end

-- Auto-load saved theme (here because applyTheme is now defined)
do
    local THEME_FILE = "sacrifice_theme_" .. tostring(LocalPlayer.UserId) .. ".txt"
    local ok, saved = pcall(readfile, THEME_FILE)
    if ok and saved then
        local tid = saved:match("^%s*(.-)%s*$")
        local VALID = { original=true, blue=true, minty=true, bw=true }
        if tid and VALID[tid] then
            task.spawn(function()
                if wlMain and applyTheme then applyTheme(tid) end
            end)
        end
    end
end

-- -- Theme dropdown UI (inline, no floating popup) ---------
local function _setupThemeDropdown()
    local themeDropRow = Instance.new("Frame")
    themeDropRow.Size = UDim2.new(1, 0, 0, 34)
    themeDropRow.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(14, 9, 9)
    themeDropRow.BorderSizePixel = 0
    themeDropRow.LayoutOrder = 1
    themeDropRow.Parent = themeScroll
    Instance.new("UICorner", themeDropRow).CornerRadius = UDim.new(0, 4)

    local themeToggleBtn = Instance.new("TextButton")
    themeToggleBtn.Size = UDim2.new(1, 0, 1, 0)
    themeToggleBtn.BackgroundTransparency = 1
    themeToggleBtn.Text = ""
    themeToggleBtn.AutoButtonColor = false
    themeToggleBtn.ZIndex = 2
    themeToggleBtn.Parent = themeDropRow

    local themeLabelLeft = Instance.new("TextLabel")
    themeLabelLeft.Size = UDim2.new(0, 80, 1, 0)
    themeLabelLeft.Position = UDim2.new(0, 12, 0, 0)
    themeLabelLeft.BackgroundTransparency = 1
    themeLabelLeft.Text = "Theme"
    themeLabelLeft.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(165, 118, 118)
    themeLabelLeft.TextSize = 11
    themeLabelLeft.Font = Enum.Font.GothamMedium
    themeLabelLeft.TextXAlignment = Enum.TextXAlignment.Left
    themeLabelLeft.ZIndex = 2
    themeLabelLeft.Parent = themeDropRow

    local themeCurrentLbl = Instance.new("TextLabel")
    themeCurrentLbl.Size = UDim2.new(0, 120, 1, 0)
    themeCurrentLbl.Position = UDim2.new(1, -148, 0, 0)
    themeCurrentLbl.BackgroundTransparency = 1
    themeCurrentLbl.Text = "Original"
    themeCurrentLbl.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(240, 210, 210)
    themeCurrentLbl.TextSize = 11
    themeCurrentLbl.Font = Enum.Font.GothamMedium
    themeCurrentLbl.TextXAlignment = Enum.TextXAlignment.Right
    themeCurrentLbl.ZIndex = 2
    themeCurrentLbl.Parent = themeDropRow

    local themeArrow = Instance.new("TextLabel")
    themeArrow.Size = UDim2.new(0, 20, 1, 0)
    themeArrow.Position = UDim2.new(1, -22, 0, 0)
    themeArrow.BackgroundTransparency = 1
    themeArrow.Text = "\xe2\x96\xbc"
    themeArrow.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(165, 118, 118)
    themeArrow.TextSize = 12
    themeArrow.Font = Enum.Font.GothamBold
    themeArrow.ZIndex = 2
    themeArrow.Parent = themeDropRow

    local THEME_ROW_H = 30
    local themeOptionsFrame = Instance.new("Frame")
    themeOptionsFrame.Size = UDim2.new(1, -8, 0, 0)
    themeOptionsFrame.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(18, 10, 10)
    themeOptionsFrame.BorderSizePixel = 0
    themeOptionsFrame.ClipsDescendants = true
    themeOptionsFrame.LayoutOrder = 2
    themeOptionsFrame.Visible = false
    themeOptionsFrame.Parent = themeScroll
    Instance.new("UICorner", themeOptionsFrame).CornerRadius = UDim.new(0, 3)
    local toStroke = Instance.new("UIStroke")
    toStroke.Color = Color3.fromRGB(44, 18, 18)
    toStroke.Thickness = 1
    toStroke.Parent = themeOptionsFrame

    local toLayout = Instance.new("UIListLayout")
    toLayout.SortOrder = Enum.SortOrder.LayoutOrder
    toLayout.Parent = themeOptionsFrame

    local themeDropOpen = false
    local function setThemeDrop(open)
        themeDropOpen = open
        local targetH = open and (#THEME_LIST * THEME_ROW_H) or 0
        if open then
            themeOptionsFrame.Size = UDim2.new(1, -8, 0, 0)
            themeOptionsFrame.Visible = true
            ts:Create(themeOptionsFrame, TweenInfo.new(0.12, Enum.EasingStyle.Quart, Enum.EasingDirection.Out),
                {Size = UDim2.new(1, -8, 0, targetH)}):Play()
        else
            local tw = ts:Create(themeOptionsFrame, TweenInfo.new(0.12, Enum.EasingStyle.Quad, Enum.EasingDirection.In),
                {Size = UDim2.new(1, -8, 0, 0)})
            tw:Play()
            tw.Completed:Connect(function() themeOptionsFrame.Visible = false end)
        end
        themeArrow.Text = open and "\xe2\x96\xbe" or "\xe2\x96\xbc"
    end

    local function _buildThemeRow(_te, _tof, _tcl, _applyT, _setDrop, _activeTheme)
        local opt = Instance.new("TextButton")
        opt.Size = UDim2.new(1, 0, 0, THEME_ROW_H)
        opt.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(18, 10, 10)
        opt.BorderSizePixel = 0
        opt.Text = ""
        opt.AutoButtonColor = false
        opt.Parent = _tof

        local optLbl = Instance.new("TextLabel")
        optLbl.Size = UDim2.new(1, -40, 1, 0)
        optLbl.Position = UDim2.new(0, 16, 0, 0)
        optLbl.BackgroundTransparency = 1
        optLbl.Text = _te.label
        optLbl.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(165, 118, 118)
        optLbl.TextSize = 11
        optLbl.Font = Enum.Font.GothamMedium
        optLbl.TextXAlignment = Enum.TextXAlignment.Left
        optLbl.Parent = opt

        local checkLbl = Instance.new("TextLabel")
        checkLbl.Name = "ThemeCheckMark"
        checkLbl.Size = UDim2.new(0, 20, 1, 0)
        checkLbl.Position = UDim2.new(1, -26, 0, 0)
        checkLbl.BackgroundTransparency = 1
        checkLbl.Text = (_activeTheme == _te.id) and "\xe2\x9c\x93" or ""
        checkLbl.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(240, 210, 210)
        checkLbl.TextSize = 12
        checkLbl.Font = Enum.Font.GothamBold
        checkLbl.Parent = opt

        local _id    = _te.id
        local _label = _te.label
        opt.MouseEnter:Connect(function() opt.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(25, 15, 15) end)
        opt.MouseLeave:Connect(function() opt.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(18, 10, 10) end)
        opt.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
            for _, c in pairs(_tof:GetChildren()) do
                if c:IsA("TextButton") then
                    local cm = c:FindFirstChild("ThemeCheckMark")
                    if cm then cm.Text = "" end
                end
            end
            checkLbl.Text = "\xe2\x9c\x93"
            _tcl.Text = _label
            _applyT(_id)
            _setDrop(false)
        end)
    end

    for i, themeEntry in ipairs(THEME_LIST) do
        _buildThemeRow(themeEntry, themeOptionsFrame, themeCurrentLbl, applyTheme, setThemeDrop, activeTheme)
    end

    themeToggleBtn.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
        setThemeDrop(not themeDropOpen)
    end)
end

_setupThemeDropdown()


-- Start on Settings tab
switchTab("target")
-- Auto-open GUI on first load (key already validated)
wlMain.Size = UDim2.new(0, 1200, 0, 0)
-- Final position already set with AnchorPoint
wlMain.Visible = true
ts:Create(wlMain, TweenInfo.new(0.128, Enum.EasingStyle.Quart, Enum.EasingDirection.Out), {Size = UDim2.new(0, 1050, 0, 700), Position = UDim2.new(0.5, 0, 0.5, -20)}):Play()

-- ============================================================
--  MAIN RENDER LOOP
-- ============================================================
-- Camera axis-masked lerp -- hoisted OUT of RenderStepped so it is allocated ONCE, not every frame
-- camPos captured as upvalue at call site; _axisMode/_axisCamPos are set before calling
local _axisCamPos   = Vector3.new(0,0,0)   -- set by camera lock code before each call
local _axisMode     = "Full"               -- set by camera lock code before each call
local function applyAxisMasked(from, to, alpha)
    if _axisMode == "Full" then
        return from:Lerp(to, alpha)
    elseif _axisMode == "Y Only" then
        local fx, fy, fz = from:ToEulerAnglesYXZ()
        local _, ty, _  = to:ToEulerAnglesYXZ()
        local ny = fy + (ty - fy) * alpha
        return CFrameNew(_axisCamPos) * CFrame.fromEulerAnglesYXZ(fx, ny, fz)
    elseif _axisMode == "X Only" then
        local fx, fy, fz = from:ToEulerAnglesYXZ()
        local tx, _, _  = to:ToEulerAnglesYXZ()
        local nx = fx + (tx - fx) * alpha
        return CFrameNew(_axisCamPos) * CFrame.fromEulerAnglesYXZ(nx, fy, fz)
    end
    return from:Lerp(to, alpha)
end



-- ============================================================
--  OTHER HEARTBEAT CONNECTIONS (speed, spider, delay)
--  Defined separately for register separation
-- ============================================================
RunService.Heartbeat:Connect(_hb_speed)
RunService.Heartbeat:Connect(_hb_spider)
RunService.Heartbeat:Connect(_hb_delay)

-- OPT: tbFindTarget throttle state wrapped in closure
local _tbCache = { scanLast = 0, cachedPart = nil }

local function _renderStepMain()
    -- OPT: cache viewport + FOV tan once per frame instead of per-branch
    local _vpSize  = Camera.ViewportSize
    local _fovTan  = math.tan(Camera.FieldOfView * 0.5 * math.pi / 180)
    
    -- Update locked target text position to bottom center of screen
    pcall(function()
        if lockedTargetText then
            lockedTargetText.Position = Vector2.new(_vpSize.X / 2, _vpSize.Y - 50)
        end
        -- Update status display (red logo + white info) - center bottom
        if statusBottomText_Logo or statusBottomText_Info then
            local logoText, infoText = getStatusText()
            if statusBottomText_Logo then
                statusBottomText_Logo.Text = logoText
                statusBottomText_Logo.Position = Vector2.new(_vpSize.X / 2, _vpSize.Y - 135)
            end
            if statusBottomText_Info then
                statusBottomText_Info.Text = infoText
                statusBottomText_Info.Position = Vector2.new(_vpSize.X / 2, _vpSize.Y - 110)
            end
        end
    end)

    if selfKnocked() then
        if not LockedTarget then
            currentTarget = nil
        end
        silentAimActive = false
        lastValidHitCF  = nil
        if not LockedTarget then
            TargetTracer.Visible = false
        end
        return  -- early exit when knocked
    end  -- closes if selfKnocked()

    -- === SILENT AIM UPDATE ===
    local _sel = SilentAimCfg["Selection"]
    local _isBoth = _sel == "Both"
    if _sel == "Target" or (_isBoth and LockedTarget) then

        local targetAlive = updateLockedTarget()
        if targetAlive then
            silentAimActive = true

            -- Advanced Camera Lock -- multi-mode, multi-axis
            if LockedTarget and currentTarget and currentTarget.Parent then
                local camLk = SilentAimCfg["Target Lock"]["Camera Follow"]
                if camLk["Enabled"] then
                    local targetPos = currentTarget.Position
                    local camPos = Camera.CFrame.Position
                    local dist = (targetPos - camPos).Magnitude

                    -- Visibility gate (optional)
                    local visOk = (not camLk["Visibility"]) or isVisible(currentTarget)

                    if dist > 1 and dist <= (camLk["Max Distance"] or 200) and visOk then
                        local mode = camLk["Mode"] or "Smooth Follow"
                        local axis = camLk["Axis"] or "Full"
                        local spd  = camLk["Speed"] or 0.15
                        local curCF = Camera.CFrame

                        -- Compute raw look CFrame toward target
                        local rawLook = CFrameNew(camPos, targetPos)

                        -- Aim Lock mode: keep target pinned to a fixed screen anchor
                        if mode == "Aim Lock" then
                            -- OPT: reuse _vpSize cached at top of RenderStepped
                            local anchorX = (camLk["Aim Screen X"] or 0.5) * _vpSize.X
                            local anchorY = (camLk["Aim Screen Y"] or 0.4) * _vpSize.Y
                            local screenPt, _, onScr = worldToViewport(targetPos)
                            if onScr then
                                local dx = screenPt.X - anchorX
                                local dy = screenPt.Y - anchorY
                                -- OPT: reuse cached _fovTan and _vpSize
                                local pitch = math.atan(dy / _vpSize.Y * 2 * _fovTan)
                                local yaw   = math.atan(dx / _vpSize.X * 2 * _fovTan * (_vpSize.X / _vpSize.Y))
                                Camera.CFrame = curCF * CFrame.Angles(-pitch * spd * 6, -yaw * spd * 6, 0)
                            end
                        else
                            -- Predictive mode: lead slightly ahead of the target's velocity
                            if mode == "Predictive" then
                                local vel = currentTarget.AssemblyLinearVelocity
                                if vel.Magnitude > 1 then
                                    rawLook = CFrameNew(camPos, targetPos + vel * 0.18)
                                end
                            end

                            -- applyAxisMasked is defined above RenderStepped (hoisted to avoid per-frame allocation)

                            if mode == "Hard Lock" then
                                _axisCamPos = camPos
                                _axisMode   = axis
                                Camera.CFrame = applyAxisMasked(curCF, rawLook, 1)
                            else -- Smooth Follow or Predictive
                                Camera.CFrame = applyAxisMasked(curCF, rawLook, spd)
                            end
                        end
                    end
                end
            end
        else
            handleRelock()
            if not LockedTargetUserId then
                silentAimActive = false
                currentTarget   = nil
                lastValidHitCF  = nil   -- FIX2: stale aim cleared when locked target lost
            end
        end

    elseif _sel == "Automatic" or (_isBoth and not LockedTarget) then
        local now = tick()
        if now - lastTargetScan >= scanRate then
            lastTargetScan = now

            local scanned = findTarget(false)
            if scanned then
                -- Valid target found -- use it and refresh stickiness
                currentTarget   = scanned
                lastValidTarget = scanned
                stickyFrames    = 0
                silentAimActive = true
            elseif lastValidTarget and lastValidTarget.Parent and stickyFrames < STICKY_MAX then
                -- Target briefly invalid -- keep last valid for a few frames
                -- Prevents intermittent misses from 1-frame flickers
                currentTarget   = lastValidTarget
                stickyFrames    = stickyFrames + 1
                silentAimActive = true
            else
                -- No valid target and stickiness expired
                currentTarget   = nil
                lastValidTarget = nil
                stickyFrames    = 0
                lastValidHitCF  = nil   -- FIX2: stale aim cleared when no target
                silentAimActive = false
            end
        end
    end

    -- === TRIGGER BOT UPDATE ===
    if TBCfg["Enabled"] and tbActive and not holdingKnife() then
        local validTarget = false

        if TBCfg["Selection"] == "Target" then
            -- Target mode: update locked target's part
            if tbLockedTarget and tbLockedTarget.Character then
                if isAlive(tbLockedTarget) and tbLockedTarget.Character and not playerKnocked(tbLockedTarget) then
                    local char = tbLockedTarget.Character
                    local hitPart = TBCfg["Hit Location"]["Hit Part"]
                    if hitPart == "Closest" then
                        tbCurrentPart = closestBodyPart(char) or char:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
                    else
                        tbCurrentPart = char:FindFirstChild(hitPart) or char:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
                    end

                    if tbCurrentPart then
                        -- Distance check
                        local myChar = LocalPlayer.Character
                        local myHRP = myChar and myChar:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
                        local tHRP = char:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
                        if myHRP and tHRP and (myHRP.Position - tHRP.Position).Magnitude <= TBCfg["Max Distance"] then
                            if not CoreChecks["Visible"] or isVisible(tbCurrentPart) then
                                validTarget = true
                            end
                        end
                    end
                end
            end
        elseif TBCfg["Selection"] == "Automatic" then
            -- Automatic mode: find closest target in FOV (~20hz throttle -- was every frame)
            local _nowTB = tick()
            if _nowTB - _tbCache.scanLast >= 0.05 then
                _tbCache.scanLast = _nowTB
                local part, _ = tbFindTarget()
                _tbCache.cachedPart = part
            end
            if _tbCache.cachedPart and _tbCache.cachedPart.Parent then
                tbCurrentPart = _tbCache.cachedPart
                validTarget = true
            end
        end

        -- Fire if we have a valid target and delay has passed AND we have ammo
        if validTarget and tbCurrentPart and tbCurrentPart.Parent then
            local now = tick()
            if now - tbLastShot >= TBCfg["Delay"] then
                -- Check ammo before firing
                local currentAmmo = getWeaponAmmo()
                if currentAmmo > 0 then
                    tbLastShot = now
                    if mouse1click then mouse1click() end
                end
            end
        end

        -- Update FOV circle position (only if visible)
        if TBCfg["FOV"]["Show FOV"] and tbFOVCircle then
            tbFOVCircle.Position = UserInputService:GetMouseLocation()
            tbFOVCircle.Radius   = TBCfg["FOV"]["Radius"]
            tbFOVCircle.Visible  = tbActive
        end
    else
        -- Hide FOV circle when TB is inactive
        if tbFOVCircle then
            tbFOVCircle.Visible = false
        end
    end

    -- Update ESP
    if ESPCfg["Enabled"] then
        updateESP()
    else
        -- When ESP is disabled, hide all drawings and clear the table
        for _p, _d in pairs(ESPObjects) do
            hideESPDrawings(_d)
        end
        -- Clear ESPObjects so fresh drawings are created when re-enabled
        ESPObjects = {}
    end
    
    updateTargetTracer()
end

RunService.RenderStepped:Connect(function()
    _renderStepMain()
end)

print("[sacrifice] loaded")


end) -- end of main pcall wrapper

if not __mainOk then
    warn("[sacrifice] SCRIPT ERROR: " .. tostring(__mainErr))
end

-- Restore Drawing.new
if _origDrawingNew then
    pcall(function() Drawing.new = _origDrawingNew end)

-- ============================================================
-- GRIP TELEPORT BULLET TP (from message(5).txt)
-- ============================================================

local function CFrameToOffset(origin, target)
    local actualOrigin = origin * CFrame.new(0,-1,0,1,0,0,0,0,1,0,-1,0)
    return actualOrigin:ToObjectSpace(target):Inverse()
end

local function TeleportBullet(tool)
    if not LockedTarget or not LockedTarget.Character then return end
    local target = LockedTarget.Character
    local targetRoot = target:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
    if not targetRoot then return end
    
    if not (lp.Character and lp.Character:FindFirstChild("RightHand")) then return end
    
    local originalGrip = tool.Grip
    tool.Parent = lp.Backpack
    tool.Grip = CFrameToOffset(lp.Character.RightHand.CFrame, targetRoot.CFrame)
    tool.Parent = lp.Character
    RunService.RenderStepped:Wait()
    tool.Parent = lp.Backpack
    tool.Grip = originalGrip
    tool.Parent = lp.Character
end

task.spawn(function()
    while true do
        task.wait(0.08)
        if WeaponModCfg["Bullet TP"] and LockedTarget then
            local tool = lp.Character and lp.Character:FindFirstChildOfClass("Tool")
            if tool then pcall(function() TeleportBullet(tool) end) end
        end
    end
end)

end

--// ============================================================
--// CLOUD CONFIG SYSTEM - FINAL FIX
--// ============================================================

local HttpService = game:GetService("HttpService")
local GITHUB_TOKEN = "ghp_YOUR_ACTUAL_TOKEN_HERE" -- <--- MAKE SURE THIS STARTS WITH ghp_

local function ExportCloudData()
    local configData = {
        Keybinds = Keybinds,
        CoreChecks = CoreChecks,
        SilentAimCfg = SilentAimCfg,
        TriggerBotCfg = TriggerBotCfg,
        WeaponModCfg = WeaponModCfg,
        SpeedCfg = SpeedCfg,
        SpiderCfg = SpiderCfg,
        InfiniteRangeCfg = InfiniteRangeCfg,
        ESPCfg = ESPCfg,
    }
    
    local function fixColors(t)
        for k, v in pairs(t) do
            if typeof(v) == "Color3" then
                t[k] = {r = v.R, g = v.G, b = v.B, _isColor = true}
            elseif typeof(v) == "table" then
                fixColors(v)
            end
        end
    end
    fixColors(configData)
    return HttpService:JSONEncode(configData)
end

local function ImportCloudData(json)
    local data = HttpService:JSONDecode(json)
    local function restoreColors(t)
        for k, v in pairs(t) do
            if typeof(v) == "table" and v._isColor then
                t[k] = Color3.new(v.r, v.g, v.b)
            elseif typeof(v) == "table" then
                restoreColors(v)
            end
        end
    end
    restoreColors(data)

    local configs = {"Keybinds", "CoreChecks", "SilentAimCfg", "TriggerBotCfg", "WeaponModCfg", "SpeedCfg", "SpiderCfg", "InfiniteRangeCfg", "ESPCfg"}
    for _, name in ipairs(configs) do
        if data[name] then
            local target = getfenv()[name] or _G[name]
            if target then
                for k, v in pairs(data[name]) do
                    target[k] = v
                end
            end
        end
    end

    for _, refresh in ipairs(toggleRefreshers) do
        pcall(refresh)
    end
end

-- UI INJECTION
local ConfigTabFrame = tabFrames["config"]
local ConfigScroll = ConfigTabFrame:FindFirstChildOfClass("ScrollingFrame")

if ConfigScroll then
    createListHeader(ConfigScroll, " CLOUD SHARING", 15)

    local shareRow = createListRow(ConfigScroll, "Generate Share Code", 16)
    local shareBtn = Instance.new("TextButton")
    shareBtn.Size = UDim2.new(0, 80, 0, 22)
    shareBtn.Position = UDim2.new(1, -90, 0.5, -11)
    shareBtn.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(35, 35, 45)
    shareBtn.Text = "SHARE"
    shareBtn.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(150, 200, 255)
    shareBtn.Font = Enum.Font.GothamBold
    shareBtn.TextSize = 10
    shareBtn.Parent = shareRow
    Instance.new("UICorner", shareBtn)

    local importRow = createListRow(ConfigScroll, "Import via Code", 17)
    local codeInput = Instance.new("TextBox")
    codeInput.Size = UDim2.new(0, 100, 0, 22)
    codeInput.Position = UDim2.new(1, -195, 0.5, -11)
    codeInput.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(20, 20, 25)
    codeInput.PlaceholderText = "Enter Code"
    codeInput.Text = ""
    codeInput.TextColor3 = Color3.new(1,1,1)
    codeInput.Font = Enum.Font.Code
    codeInput.TextSize = 10
    codeInput.Parent = importRow
    Instance.new("UICorner", codeInput)

    local loadBtn = Instance.new("TextButton")
    loadBtn.Size = UDim2.new(0, 80, 0, 22)
    loadBtn.Position = UDim2.new(1, -90, 0.5, -11)
    loadBtn.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(45, 35, 35)
    loadBtn.Text = "LOAD"
    loadBtn.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(255, 150, 150)
    loadBtn.Font = Enum.Font.GothamBold
    loadBtn.TextSize = 10
    loadBtn.Parent = importRow
    Instance.new("UICorner", loadBtn)

    -- THE PART THAT FIXES THE JSON ISSUE
    shareBtn.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
        if GITHUB_TOKEN == "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" or #GITHUB_TOKEN < 10 then
            shareBtn.Text = "SET TOKEN!"
            return
        end

        shareBtn.Text = "UPLOADING..."
        local rawJson = ExportCloudData()
        
        local reqFunc = (syn and syn.request) or (http and http.request) or http_request or request
        local success, response = pcall(function()
            return reqFunc({
                Url = "https://api.github.com/gists",
                Method = "POST",
                Headers = {
                    ["Authorization"] = "Bearer " .. GITHUB_TOKEN,
                    ["Content-Type"] = "application/json"
                },
                Body = HttpService:JSONEncode({
                    description = "Sacrifice CC Config",
                    public = true,
                    files = { ["sacrifice.json"] = { content = rawJson } }
                })
            })
        end)

        if success and response.StatusCode == 201 then
            local data = HttpService:JSONDecode(response.Body)
            setclipboard(data.id) -- ONLY COPIES THE SHORT ID
            shareBtn.Text = "COPIED ID!"
            task.delay(2, function() shareBtn.Text = "SHARE" end)
        else
            shareBtn.Text = "ERR: CHECK CONSOLE"
            print("FAILED! Status:", response and response.StatusCode)
            print("Response Body:", response and response.Body)
            -- If it fails, it might copy the JSON as a backup. We want to stop that.
        end
    end)

    loadBtn.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
        local code = codeInput.Text
        if #code < 10 then loadBtn.Text = "SHORT CODE"; return end
        
        loadBtn.Text = "FETCHING..."
        local reqFunc = (syn and syn.request) or (http and http.request) or http_request or request
        local success, response = pcall(function()
            return reqFunc({
                Url = "https://api.github.com/gists/" .. code,
                Method = "GET"
            })
        end)

        if success and response.StatusCode == 200 then
            local gistData = HttpService:JSONDecode(response.Body)
            if gistData.files and gistData.files["sacrifice.json"] then
                ImportCloudData(gistData.files["sacrifice.json"].content)
                loadBtn.Text = "SUCCESS!"
            else
                loadBtn.Text = "FILE ERROR"
            end
            task.delay(2, function() loadBtn.Text = "LOAD" end)
        else
            loadBtn.Text = "NOT FOUND"
        end
    end)
end
